> *   `Added in some places` `**normal**` `unsuccessful` `**output**` `instead of` `**console errors**` `in` [`**entitiesInRadius**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius)
>     `,` [`**item**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
>     `,` [`**entity**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)
>      `and` [`**repeat**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text)
>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `Fixed that targets with` `**underscores**` `at the nickname start were not being` `**correctly proceed**` `in` [`**item**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
>      `and` [`**entity**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)
>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `Lore lines are` `**no**` `longer being` `**trimmed**` `in` [`**change_item**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
>      `action;`
>     
> *   `Lore outputting is` `**no**` `longer have` `**unnecessary**` `specified` `**separator**` `at its end in` [`**item**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `**Brackets**` `and` `**multiple conditions**` `now are being parsed` `**correctly**` `in` [`**array**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)
>      `and` [`**list**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)
>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `**AND**` `and` `**OR**` `delimiters are` `**no**` `longer being` `**counted**` `inside placeholders in` [`**array**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)
>      `and` [`**list**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)
>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `Symbols like` `**$**``,` `**@**``, delimiters` `**AND**``,` `**OR**` `and operators like` `**<=**``,` `**==**``,` `contains` `etc in array itself are` `**no**` `longer` `**interfere**` `conditions in` [`**array**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)
>      `placeholder;`
>     
> *   `Conditions with` `**condition operators**` `as part of the` `**expression**` `and not as condition operator now are being parsed` `**correctly**` `in` [`**array**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)
>      `placeholder;`
>     
> *   `The` [`**manage_mysql**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql)
>      `action,` [`**MySQL**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql)
>      `placeholder and` `**realUUID**` `option in` [`**entity**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)
>      `placeholders are` `**no**` `longer` `**print stacktrace**` `while encountering with errors;`
>     
> *   `The` `**ASYNC**` `mode in` [`**MySQL**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql)
>      `placeholder now returns "``**Loading...**``" when loads the data instead of` `**non-parsing placeholder**` `and puts errors as output on occassions as well.`
>     
> 
> **UPDATED:**
> 
> *   `Updated` [`**manage_inventory**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory)
>      `action: rewritten` `**code**``, fixed` `**bugs**``, added new` `**possibilities**``, improved` `**structure**``, logic and` `**functioning**``.`

>      `placeholders;`
>     
> *   `New` `**SYNC**``/``**FORCESYNC**``/``**ASYNC**``/``**FORCEASYNC**` `switching, different` `**settings**` `for them and new call event` `**variables**` `in` [`**manage_cycle**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle)
>      `action;`
>     
> *   `New` `**SYNC**``/``**ASYNC**` `switching in` [`**array**`](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)

# Installation or updation | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#installation)

Installation:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#main-plugin)

Main plugin

Install the `TriggerReactor` plugin [**here**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/TriggerReactor/TriggerReactor/releases/download/3.5.0.6-Beta/TriggerReactor-bukkit-latest-3.5.0.6-Beta.jar)
;

triangle-exclamation

**DO NOT PAY ATTENTION ON THE TEXT BELOW IF YOU ARE A REGULAR USER WHICH DOES NOT ENCOUNTER ANY PROBLEMS.**

**Only for those who know what they are doing!** Use [this versionarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/TriggerReactor/releases/download/PaperClassLoaderFixes/TriggerReactor-bukkit-latest-3.5.0.6-Beta.jar)
 to fix the Paper incorrect commands bug (**this is EXPERIMENTAL version, please report all bugs**).

2

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#dependency-plugin)

Dependency plugin

Install the `TriggerReactor` dependency [**here**arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/jshader.93342/download?version=406835)
**;**

3

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#downloading-the-addon)

Downloading the addon

Download the newest version [**here**arrow-up-right](https://akcel.fun/ce-aapp)
 OR download all source content as archive on [**GitHub**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP)
;

4

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#setting-the-addon)

Setting the addon

Unpack the contents of the archive into the plugins folder (as a result, the **plugins folder** should contain the `TriggerReactor` folder with all its contents);

5

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#restarting)

Restarting

Restart the server;

6

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#final-checking)

Final checking

Make sure that everything is installed without errors: in the console you should see messages from `ConditionalEvents` and `PlaceholderAPI` about **successful registration** of new `actions` and new `expansion` respectively.

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#updation)

Updation:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#downloading-the-addon-1)

Downloading the addon

Download the newest version [**here**arrow-up-right](https://akcel.fun/ce-aapp)
 OR download all source content as archive on [**GitHub**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP)
;

2

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#deleting)

Deleting

Delete your previous `TriggerReactor` folder;

3

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#setting-the-addon-1)

Setting the addon

Unpack the contents of the archive into the plugins folder (as a result, the **plugins folder** should contain the `TriggerReactor` folder with all its contents);

4

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#restarting-1)

Restarting

Restart the server;

5

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#final-checking-1)

Final checking

Make sure that everything is installed without errors: in the console you should see messages from `ConditionalEvents` and `PlaceholderAPI` about **successful registration** of new `actions` and new `expansion` respectively.

# Starting information | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

👋 Hello, this **addon** adds a big pack of new **actions** and **placeholders** to `ConditionalEvents`, with it you have **full control** over entities, players, storages and many other useful features: everything that was previously possible only through vanilla commands or **not possible at all** in `ConditionalEvents`, is **now possible** directly in the built-in **actions** or **placeholders**.

The **main goal** of the addon is to provide as **much functionality** as possible in addition to the existing one, **quality** tries not to be inferior to **quantity**.

* * *

circle-check

**❗Join the original** [**ConditionalEvents Discord**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/698332177137401987/1348313697436569733)
 **to the origin of this addon.**

triangle-exclamation

⚠️ Please report any problems or bugs you find, and suggest ideas for new features (to "[Issuesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP/issues)
" on GitHub, "[Discussionarrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/threads/conditionalevents-actions-and-placeholders-pack-ce-aapp.685662/)
" or [direct messagesarrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/conversations/)
 on Spigot or [direct messagesarrow-up-right](https://discordapp.com/users/440067456229179393)
 in Discord).

[PreviousLatest updateschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5)
[NextInstallation or updationchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation)

# Logical notations | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

*   (MANDATORY) – must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder;
    
*   (SEMI-MANDATORY) – must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, the current value does not need to be specified, but if it is specified in the required value, it is necessary);
    
*   (SEMI-OPTIONAL) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, it is not necessary to specify the current value, and if it is specified in the required value, it can be specified optionally);
    
*   (SEMI-OPTIONAL | SEMI-MANDATORY) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified to some value, or must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified to some another value (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, it is not necessary to specify the current value, but if it is specified in the required value, it is necessary);
    
*   (OPTIONAL) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder.
    

[PreviousInstallation or updationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation)

# change_balance | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ESSENTIALSX**arrow-up-right](https://essentialsx.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#meaning)

Allows you to change the balance of EssentialsX players using subtraction, multiplication, division operations and so on. Offline players are also supported.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#format)

Copy

    - 'change_balance: <player>;<amount>;<operation>'

<player> – the player to change the balance; (MANDATORY)

<amount> – the amount to change the balance; (MANDATORY)

<operation> – may be SET, ADD, REMOVE, MULTIPLY, DIVIDE or RESET. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to change a player's balance without using Essentials commands (to avoid displaying a feedback message in some cases and so on).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#examples)

* * *

[PreviousPlugins actionschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions)
[Nextchange\_oraxen\_blockchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_balance: %player%;1000;SET' # Set the specified player's current balance to 1000

Copy

    - 'change_balance: %player%;3;DIVIDE' # Divide the specified player's current balance by 3

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_spectating | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**PROTOCOLLIB**arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/protocollib.1997/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#meaning)

Allows you to change the spectation target of the specified player, leaving him on his real place, that is the player will spectate to the specified target like with the "/spectate" command or left-click in spectator gamemode, but the difference will be that you do not have to be in spectator gamemode and your in-game person will leave on his current place, while you will spectating.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#format)

Copy

    - 'change_spectating: <player>;<entity_uuid|player_name>'

<player> – the player for which change the spectation target; (MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the spectation target (you can use the same player to return his view). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to force some player to spectate to some entity simultaneously leaving him on his current place and leaving him exposed to any damage etc, like he is not spectating currently.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#examples)

* * *

[Previousshow\_end\_creditschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/show_end_credits)
[NextEvents actionschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions)

Last updated 6 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_spectating: %player%;c76bf00c-84f6-4556-99dc-eafec4ab847d' # Change the spectation target of the current player to some entity

# drop_items_adder_item | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ITEMSADDER**arrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#meaning)

Allows you to drop the items from the ItemsAdder plugin at a specified location not only with the /iadrop command in the ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#format)

Copy

    - 'drop_items_adder_item: <world,x,y,z>;<item_id>'

<world,x,y,z> – the location to drop the item; (MANDATORY)

<item\_id> – the item id to drop (in format namespace:id, check [itarrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.devs.beer/plugin-usage/beginners/configs-and-resourcepack#what-is-a-namespace)
 for more info). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#targets)

*   ItemsAdder items.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#where-is-useful)

For example, if you only need to use built-in actions and not third-party commands, then you could use this action to drop an item from the ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#examples)

* * *

Copy

    - 'drop_items_adder_item: world,14,64,123;customitems:pickaxe' # Drop the some custom pickaxe at the specified location

# change_items_adder_block | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ITEMSADDER**arrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#meaning)

Allows you to place and remove blocks from the ItemsAdder plugin at a specified location, since there are not any commands in ItemsAdder for that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: <mode>;<world,x,y,z>;(semi-mandatory) <block_id>'

<mode> – may be SET or REMOVE, the "SET" will place the block, and the "REMOVE" will break the block if it will be an ItemsAdder block; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location to change the block; (MANDATORY)

<block\_id> – the block id to place (only in case of "SET" mode, in format namespace:id, check [itarrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.devs.beer/plugin-usage/beginners/configs-and-resourcepack#what-is-a-namespace)
 for more info). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#targets)

*   ItemsAdder blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to place or break some blocks from ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#examples)

* * *

[Previouschange\_oraxen\_blockchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block)
[Nextdrop\_items\_adder\_itemchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: SET;world,14,64,123;customblocks:furnace' # Place the some custom furnace at the specified location

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: REMOVE;world,14,64,123' # Break the some custom block at the specified location

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_projectile | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**THIS ACTION ONLY WORKS WHEN USING** [**EntityShootBowEvent**arrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/event/entity/EntityShootBowEvent.html)
 **EVENT.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#meaning)

Allows you to change the projectile when shooting from a bow, crossbow, etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#format)

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: <projectile_type|projectile_uuid>'

<projectile\_type | projectile\_uuid> – the UUID of already existed projectile or the type of some new projectile, like Snowball or Arrow (you can find valid projectile types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Projectile.html)
, but not all of them will work). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#targets)

*   Any [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
     which firing the event by shooting from the bow.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create an apocalypse by making everyone shoot fireballs, or, conversely, create a prank by turning projectiles into llama spit.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#examples)

* * *

circle-info

Please note that by specifying the UUID of any lying item, the projectile will in any case be changed to an dirt item.

[PreviousEvents actionschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions)
[NextIndependent actionschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: Fireball' # Change the projectile to a fireball

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: d32893e0-c22b-41a6-8d74-ea785a1975ea' # Change the projectile to a some existing projectile (for example, Enderpearl)

# change_chat | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat#meaning)

Allows you to change the current player chat (clear it and set to some message).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat#format)

Copy

    - 'change_chat: <player>;<action>;(semi-mandatory) <message>'

<player> – the player to change the chat for; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be SET or CLEAR; (MANDATORY)

<message> – the message to set, you can use [JSONarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.tools/en/json_text.php)
 and [MiniMessagearrow-up-right](https://docs.advntr.dev/minimessage/format.html)
 as well as the default string (only in case of "SET" action). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to clear the current player chat or set it to some one message.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_chat: %player%;CLEAR' # Clear the current player chat

Copy

    - 'change_chat: %player%;SET;&cThe chat has been cleared!' # Set the current player chat to the some message

# change_oraxen_block | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ORAXEN**arrow-up-right](https://oraxen.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#meaning)

Allows you to place and remove blocks from the Oraxen plugin at a specified location, since there are not any commands in Oraxen for that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: <mode>;<world,x,y,z>;<block_id|forceDrop (true|false)>;(semi-optional) <player>'

<mode> – may be SET or REMOVE, the "SET" will place the block, and the "REMOVE" will break the block if it will be an Oraxen block; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location to change the block; (MANDATORY)

<block\_id | forceDrop> – the block id to place (only in case of "SET" mode) or the forceDrop state, that is, whether to force the block to drop, even if player is null or in creative mode (only in case of "REMOVE" mode). (MANDATORY)

<player> – the player who caused the block to break (only in case of "REMOVE" mode, but can be skipped). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#targets)

*   Oraxen blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to place or break some blocks from Oraxen.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#examples)

* * *

[Previouschange\_balancechevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance)
[Nextchange\_items\_adder\_blockchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: SET;world,14,64,123;customblocks:workbench' # Place the some custom workbench at the specified location

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: REMOVE;world,14,64,123;true;%player%' # Break the some custom block at the specified location with a forced drop and as if said player had done it

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_block | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#meaning)

Allows you to place the block fake or really at the specified location, or to send the fake block damaging animation to the specified player. In case of placing the fake block, it will not change the world in any way, it will only be visible to the specified player.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_block: <action>;<world,x,y,z>;<block_material|damage_progress>;(semi-optional) <player>;(semi-optional) <entity_uuid>'

<action> – may be damage or place, the "damage" will send the fake block damaging animation to the specified player, and the "place" allows you to choose whether to place the real block or fake at the specified location; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location of the block to change; (MANDATORY)

<block\_material | damage\_progress> – the material of the new block or the damage progress of the block from 0.0 to 1.0 (depends on the chosen action, see the table below); (MANDATORY)

<player> – if you want to send the fake block changes, which will not change the world in any way and only be visible to the specified player, specify the player (the need to specify depends on the chosen action, see the table below); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

<entity\_uuid> – in case of "damage" action, you can specify the entity which will be source of this block damage. (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#table-of-required-options-for-different-actions-checkmarks-or-text-are-what-must-necessarily-be-used)

Table of required options for different actions (checkmarks or text are what must necessarily be used (or optional if specified)):

ACTION

<world,x,y,z>

<block\_material | damage\_progress>

<player>

<entity\_uuid>

damage

check

block\_material

check

(optional)

place

check

damage\_progress

check

check

(optional)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#targets)

*   Any blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to make a player crawl, you can place fake barriers over him that will only affect him. Or you can send a fake block breaking animation to a player to troll him or something else.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_block#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_block: place;%player_world%,%player_x%,%player_y%,%player_z%;STONE' # Change a real block at the specified location to stone

Copy

    - 'change_block: damage;%player_world%,%player_x%,%math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-1%,%player_z%;0.5;%player%' # Display block damaging animation under player with progress 0.5

Copy

    - 'change_block: place;%player_world%,%player_x%,%player_y%,%player_z%;DIRT;%player%' # Change a block to the dirt at a specified location for a specified player only (that is, only visually for that player, without changing the game world)

* * *

[Previouschange\_chatchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat)
[Nextchange\_AIchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai)

# manage_inventory | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**THE ACTION IS UNDER RECONSTRUCTION CURRENTLY, TO GET RID OF BUGS, IMPROVE IMPLEMENTATION AND PROVIDE NEW USEFUL THINGS. THE CURRENT VARIANT IS UNSTABLE.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#meaning)

Allows you to save, open and delete the different inventories to the players (you can save and delete any inventories, but open only suitable of them for players).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#format)

Copy

    - 'manage_inventory: action:<action>;<option>:<value>;<optionN>:<valueN>'

action:<action> – may be save, open or delete, you can add "?" symbol before the action to use the temporary inventories storage, that is, until server restart; (MANDATORY)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#options-any-order)

Options (any order):

inventory:<inventory\_id> – indicates by which id/name the inventory will be used (can be skipped only in case of "open" action); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

fake:<true | false> – whether to open the fake inventory or not in cases of anvil, workbench and so on inventories (use only in case of "open" action, can be skipped); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

owner:<entity\_uuid | player\_name | world,x,y,z> – indicates which inventory will be used (for example of some player), if specified, all other properties will be ignored, you also can use "^" before the nickname to use the open player's inventory and "|<slot (indices or named slots)>" after to get inventory of the some item (for example, shulker box) (use only in case of "save" or "open" actions, can be skipped); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

holder:<entity\_uuid | player\_name | world,x,y,z> – the holder which will hold the inventory (use only in case of "save" or "open" actions, can be skipped); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

target:<player> – for which player the inventory will be opened (use only in case of "open" action); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

typeOrSize:<inventory\_type | integer\_size> – the type or the size of the inventory, see the available types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/event/inventory/InventoryType.html)
, in case of size it should be a multiple of 9 between 9 and 54 slots, for example, 18 (use only in case of "save" or "open" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

title:<inventory\_title> – the title of the inventory (use only in case of "open" action, can be skipped). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

The perpetual inventories and temporary inventories are different! The same inventories names will point to different inventories.

circle-exclamation

If you want to open plyer's inventory with armor contents, you firstly need to save it, then open the saved inventory.

triangle-exclamation

You can not create the "CREATIVE", "CRAFTING" and "MERCHANT" inventory types, only if specified <owner> will be merchant inventory, you can open it, but not save. You can specify the <owner> option and saving or opening inventories of this owner, without necessity to specify the inventory options like <holder>, <typeOrSize> and <title>. You can save and open any block inventories but only [InventoryHoldersarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/InventoryHolder.html)
 of them will be saving their contents. Not all mobs inventories are suitable for opening to the players due to their incompatible size. You can specify or <inventory> option to open/resave/delete the saved inventory, or <owner> option to open/save the someone's inventory, or <holder>, <typeOrSize> and <title> options to create and open/save the new inventory depends on these values.

circle-info

If "?" prefix will not be specified in the action, the inventory will be stored in a file at the path plugins/TriggerReactor/inventories.json (you can change this file, changes will take effect after the command /trg reload confirm), otherwise the inventory will be stored in the server memory until it is restarted.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#targets)

*   Entities ([InventoryHoldersarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/InventoryHolder.html)
    );
    
*   Players;
    
*   Storages ([InventoryHoldersarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/InventoryHolder.html)
    ).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to create the custom system of "virtual personal storages", it also can be combined in a useful way with [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action for "expandable storages" etc.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_inventory#examples)

* * *

[PreviousIndependent actionschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions)
[Nextchange\_chatchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_chat)

Last updated 6 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'manage_inventory: action:open;target:%player%;holder:%player%;typeOrSize:CHEST;title:§fMy little inventory' # Open the new inventory to the current player with type "CHEST", title "§fMy little inventory" and holder as the current player

Copy

    - 'manage_inventory: action:save;inventory:%player% Enderchest;owner:^%player%;title:§aSaved Enderchest' # Save the open inventory (for example, enderchest) of the current player with custom title

Copy

    - 'manage_inventory: action:open;owner:world,3097,65,8607|0;target:%player%' # Open the inventory of the item (for example, of the shulker box) in the block (for example, in the chest) at the specified location to the current player

# change_time | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_time#meaning)

Allows you to change the time for both the world and the player (that is, both global time and personal time for players).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_time#format)

Copy

    - 'change_time: <world>;<time>;(optional) <player>;(semi-optional) sync;(semi-optional) relative'

<world> – the world to change the time in (will be ignored if "player" is specified); (MANDATORY)

<time> – the time in ticks (from 0 to 24000) or DAY, NIGHT, MIDDAY or MIDNIGHT; (MANDATORY)

<player> – if you need to set the time only for the specified player; (OPTIONAL)

sync – if you need to synchronize the player's time with the server, should be just "sync" if you want to specify it or nothing otherwise (use only in case of specifying the "player"); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

relative – if need the player's time to move and not stand still, should be just "relative" if you want to specify it or nothing otherwise (use only in case of specifying the "player"). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-info

"Sync" and "relative" options may be specified in any order and any of them may be skipped.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_time#targets)

*   Global time;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_time#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to change the time for world or player using built-in actions and not commands from other plugins like EssentialsX.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_time#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_time: world;DAY' # Set the time to "DAY" in the world "world"

Copy

    - 'change_time: world;15000;%player%;relative' # Set the time to "15000" to the current player and make it move and not stand still

* * *

[Previouschange\_weatherchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather)
[Nextchange\_freezechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_freeze)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_AI | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai#meaning)

If you turn off an entity's AI, it will not interact with the world in any way, but will still be susceptible to damage.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai#format)

Copy

    - 'change_AI: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<true|false>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the AI; (MANDATORY)

<true|false> – whether to enable or disable the AI. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai#targets)

*   [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
    ;
    
*   Players (this is possible, but players are not affected by AI for real).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai#where-is-useful)

For example, if you are creating some sort of challenge or mini game where the player is defending against enemy mobs, and the player has the ability to “freeze” certain mobs.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ai#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_AI: 9926220f-475c-43b4-870a-024a1f6b7bed;false' # Disable the AI of some entity

# change_fire | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire#meaning)

Allows you to set the entities on fire (visually and real).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire#format)

Copy

    - 'change_fire: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<duration>;(optional) <visual (true|false)>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the fire; (MANDATORY)

<duration> – the duration of the fire in ticks; (MANDATORY)

<visual> – the state whether to enable or disable the visual fire (duration will be ignored if you specify this option). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to ignite or extinguish the entities visually or real.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_fire: dfeafd16-b87d-4315-ba27-6d721e9107b4;100;false' # Ignite the specified entity to the 100 ticks (5 seconds)

Copy

    - 'change_fire: %player%;20;true' # Ignite the current player visually (the duration is ignored)

* * *

# change_weather | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather#meaning)

Allows you to change the weather.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather#format)

Copy

    - 'change_weather: <world>;<weather_type>;(optional) <duration>'

<world> – the world to change the weather in; (MANDATORY)

<weather\_type> – the weather type, may be SUN, STORM or THUNDER; (MANDATORY)

<duration> – the duration of the weather in seconds. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather#targets)

*   Weather.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to change the weather using built-in actions and not commands.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_weather#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_weather: world;STORM' # Set the weather to "STORM" in the world "world"

Copy

    - 'change_weather: world;THUNDER;60' # Set the weather to "THUNDER" in the world "world" to 60 seconds

* * *

# change_gravity | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity#meaning)

Allows you to change the gravity of the entities, that is, the entities will not falling (but they also will not take off, you need to use [change\_effect](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect)
 action for that to give the levitation effect).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity#format)

Copy

    - 'change_gravity: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<gravity (true|false)>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the gravity; (MANDATORY)

<gravity> – the state to change the gravity to. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create some mini-game with some certain possibilites, like this.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_gravity: %player%;false' # Disable the gravity to the current player

* * *

# create_explosion | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#meaning)

Allows you to create the customizable explosions like spawning different TNTs or performing instant explosions.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#format)

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: <world>;<x>;<y>;<z>;<type>;<power>;(semi-mandatory) <delay>;(semi-mandatory) <set_fire (true|false)>;(semi-mandatory) <break_blocks (true|false)>;(semi-optional) <source_entity (entity_uuid|player_name)>'

<world>;<x>;<y>;<z> – the location to create the explosion; (MANDATORY)

<type> – may be TNT or EXPLOSION; (MANDATORY)

<power> – the power of the explosion (can be in float); (MANDATORY)

<delay> – the delay before the explosion in ticks (only in case of "TNT" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<set\_fire> – whether to make the blocks on fire after the explosion or not (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<break\_blocks> – whether to break the blocks after the explosion or not (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<source\_entity> – the entity which caused the explosion (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type, can be skipped). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#table-of-required-options-for-different-types-checkmarks-are-what-must-necessarily-be-used-or-option)

Table of required options for different types (checkmarks are what must necessarily be used (or optional if specified)):

TYPE

<world>;<x>;<y>;<z>

<power>

<delay>

<set\_fire>

<break\_blocks>

<source\_entity>

TNT

check

check

check

EXPLOSION

check

check

check

check

check

(optional)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Options that are not needed for one <type> or another should be completely skipped, and not just left empty.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#targets)

*   Locations.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create some apocalypse and blowing everything up, or create pretty popular "tnt-sheep" which will be blowed after some time of living.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#examples)

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: world;52;64;634;TNT;10;100' # Spawn the tnt at the specified location with 10 explosive power and 100 ticks (5 seconds) delay before the explosion

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: world;52;64;634;EXPLOSION;10;true;true;%player%' # Create the explosion at the specified location with 10 explosive power, making the blocks on fire and breaking them, using the current player as the source of the explosion

[Previouschange\_firechevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fire)
[Nextchange\_gravitychevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# parse_placeholder | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder#meaning)

Allows you to parse a placeholder without any output. Actually does nothing, because placeholders are parsing in ConditionalEvents, and exactly the main thing of this action is doing nothing.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder#format)

Copy

    - 'parse_placeholder: <placeholder>'

<placeholder> – the placeholder to parse. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder#targets)

*   Any.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder#where-is-useful)

For example, if you have placeholders which changing some data and not obtaining it, like JavaScript placeholders from PlaceholderAPI or [customData](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data)
 placeholder in some cases, and you need to use them in a comfortable way.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder#examples)

Copy

    - 'parse_placeholder: %CEP_customData_set_coins_2_{player}%' # Parse customData placeholder to just set the value

* * *

[Previouschange\_gravitychevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gravity)
[Nextchange\_speedchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed)

# change_invulnerable | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_invulnerable#meaning)

Allows you to change the invulnerability of the entities, that is they will not be able to take the damage.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_invulnerable#format)

Copy

    - 'change_invulnerable: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<mode>;<value>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the invulnerable for; (MANDATORY)

<mode> – may be invulnerable or noDamageTicks; (MANDATORY)

<value> – "true" or "false" in case of "invulnerable" mode or ticks duration in case of "noDamageTicks" mode. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_invulnerable#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_invulnerable#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create some kind of "newbies protection" when the new players are joining to the server.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_invulnerable#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_invulnerable: e2b4de9b-be7b-4058-86b0-04ac31195db1;invulnerable;true' # Enable the invulnerability to some entity

Copy

    - 'change_invulnerable: %player%;noDamageTicks;100' # Disable the damage for the 100 ticks (5 seconds) to the current player

* * *

[Previouschange\_glidingchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding)
[Nextchange\_visibilitychevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_visibility)

# change_speed | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed#meaning)

Allows you to change the flying and walking speed of the players.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed#format)

Copy

    - 'change_speed: <player>;<mode>;<speed>'

<player> – the player to change the speed for; (MANDATORY)

<mode> – may be WALK or FLY; (MANDATORY)

<speed> – the speed to change to (from -1.0 to 1.0). (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-info

The default player walking speed is 0.2 and flying speed is 0.1. By setting flying speed to the negative values you are inverting the movements (like forward moving will actually move you backward).

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to change the player speed using built-in actions and not commands from other plugins like EssentialsX (and even EssentialsX speed commands are not allowing you to use negative values).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_speed#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_speed: %player%;WALK;0.5' # Increase the current player walking speed to 0.5

Copy

    - 'change_speed: %player%;FLY;-0.9' # Increase the current player flying speed and inverting it

* * *

[Previousparse\_placeholderchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/parse_placeholder)
[Nextchange\_ticks\_livedchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# change_ticks_lived | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived#meaning)

Allows you to change the lifespan of the entities in ticks, that is, the time, for which entity is already living from the spawn moment.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived#format)

Copy

    - 'change_ticks_lived: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<ticks>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the lived ticks for; (MANDATORY)

<ticks> – the ticks of the new lifespan of the entity (strictly more than 1). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in some technical systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_ticks_lived: 9926220f-475c-43b4-870a-024a1f6b7bed;25000' # Change the lived ticks of some entity to the 25000

# change_experience | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience#meaning)

Allows you to change players experience bar by percentage, that is it does not matter what level player has, this action will set the percentage of the current experience bar fullness.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience#format)

Copy

    - 'change_experience: <player_name>;<action>;<value>'

<player\_name> – the player to change the experience for; (MANDATORY)

<action> – the action to perform on the experience, may be SET, ADD, REMOVE, MULTIPLY, DIVIDE or RESET; (MANDATORY)

<value> – the value itself. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience#targets)

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience#where-is-useful)

Wherever you will need to implement such mechanic with percentage experience bar, for example in some minigames and other systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_experience: %player%;ADD;40' # Add 40 percents to the current experience bar of the current player

# launch_projectile | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/launch_projectile#meaning)

Allows you to launch the projectiles from the entities, as if they were launching them.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/launch_projectile#format)

Copy

    - 'launch_projectile: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<projectile_type>;(optional) <velocity_x,velocity_y,velocity_z>;(semi-optional) <relative_x,relative_y,relative_z (true|false)>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to launch the projectile from; (MANDATORY)

<projectile\_type> – the type of some new projectile, like Snowball or Arrow (you can find valid projectile types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Projectile.html)
, but not all of them will work); (MANDATORY)

<velocity\_x,velocity\_y,velocity\_z> – the velocity of the projectile in each direction; (OPTIONAL)

<relative\_x,relative\_y,relative\_z> – the relative state of the each direction velocity, should be "true" or "false" for each direction, that is, whether the player view direction will be used or the default world direction (only in case of specifying the "velocity\_x,velocity\_y,velocity\_z"). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/launch_projectile#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/launch_projectile#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to make some special mobs in some mini-game (bosses or supporters) which will be sometimes shot with arrows or fireballs, or vice versa with something useful like experience bottles.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/launch_projectile#examples)

Copy

    - 'launch_projectile: %player%;Arrow' # Launch the arrow from the current player with the default velocity at the player view direction

Copy

    - 'launch_projectile: 6b8a2bd8-fc3f-4c83-a92b-df5bd0fc9f1a;Snowball;5,1,5;true,false,true' # Launch the snowball from the some entity with the 5 X and Z velocity and 1 Y velocity at the entity view direction

* * *

[Previouschange\_ticks\_livedchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_ticks_lived)

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_color#meaning)

Allows you to change color of the entities and blocks, for example signs, sheeps or shulkers.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_color#format)

Copy

    - 'change_color: <entity_uuid|world,x,y,z>;<color>;(semi-optional) <side>'

<entity\_uuid | world,x,y,z> – the target to change the color for; (MANDATORY)

<color> – the new color, see possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/DyeColor.html)
; (MANDATORY)

<side> – the side of the block, see possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/sign/Side.html)
 (only in case of SIGN blocks, can be skipped to use the FRONT side by default). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

# change_movement | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#meaning)

Allows you to change the different movement states of the entities (sneaking, sprinting etc).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#format)

Copy

    - 'change_movement: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<action>;<value>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the movement for; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be sprint, sneak, swim, sit or rotate; (MANDATORY)

<value> – the value to change the movement to ("true" or "false" in all actions except "rotate" action in which "yaw,pitch" as float values). (MANDATORY)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

Note that if the entity is affected by AI currently, the "rotate" option may not work pretty well, that is rotation may be overwrited by the path finding behavior almost immediately.

circle-exclamation

The "sneak" action is only visible to other players and not you, and the speed is not changing to slower. The "sprint" action is just the sprinting particles underfoot and sounds. The "swim" action does not change anything visually, it just changes the swimming state for a one tick. The "sit" action is only applicable to the sittable entities like dogs.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#targets)

*   [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
    ;
    
*   [Sittablesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Sittable.html)
    ;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to change different movement states of the entities.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_movement: %player%;sneak;true' # Force the current player to sneak visually for other players

Copy

    - 'change_movement: 1548f301-d23d-4655-8e20-2e41905784dc;rotate;52,-27' # Force some entity to rotate in specified yaw and pitch

* * *

[Previouschange\_colorchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_color)
[Nextchange\_namechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name)

Last updated 8 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_visibility | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

Copy

<player\_name> – the player to which change the visibility of the entities; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be HIDE or SHOW; (MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuids | player\_names> – the entities through the comma to change the visibility for, entities available only from 1.18+, otherwise only players are available. (MANDATORY)

# change_destination | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination#meaning)

Allows you to modify entities and players path finding, that is you can force entities and players moving somewhere finding the best way.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination#format)

Copy

    - 'change_destination: <action>;<entity_uuid|player_name>;(semi-mandatory) <target_uuid|player_name|world,x,y,z>;(semi-mandatory) <modify_view (true|false)>;(semi-mandatory) <ignore_flying (true|false)>;(semi-mandatory) <continue_after_stop (true|false)>;(semi-optional) <speed>'

<action> – may be SET or RESET; (MANDATORY)

(CONTAINS EXPERIMENTAL FEATURES) <entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the entity to change the destination for `**(see the hint for more imortant info)**`; (MANDATORY)

<target\_uuid | player\_name | world,x,y,z> – the target location or entity for the destination; (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<modify\_view> – whether to lock the view direction when moving or leave it free (recommended for reduce moving interference) **(only in case of "SET" action)** `**(see the hint for more imortant info)**`; (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<ignore\_flying> – whether to ignore flying possibilities of the entity or not, that is if the entity can fly and currently flying, this option will move entity even in the air if set to "true" (recommended for normal moving of the flying entities too), otherwise it will move entity only if it is on the ground **(only in case of "SET" action)** `**(see the hint for more imortant info)**`; (SEMI-MANDATORY)

(EXPERIMENTAL) <continue\_after\_stop> – whether to renew the path finding if previously was ended or not, because for large distances the path finding can ending before final point **(only in case of "SET" action)** `**(see the hint for more imortant info)**`; (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<speed> – the speed of the moving, can be in float values, for entities which are not a Mobs (**see more in the hint**) the normal speed is 0.2 and sneaking (lower) speed is 0.1 (**too high (above 1.0) or too low (below 0.05) speeds are not recommended**), and for entities which are a Mobs (**see more in the hint**) the normal speed is 1.0 and sneaking (lower) speed is 0.5 (**too high (above 2.0) or too low (below 0.5) speeds are not recommended**) **(only in case of "SET" action, but optionally)**; (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**Not all options support all entity types!** The <modify\_view> and <ignore\_flying> options are support any entities which are not a [Mobarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Mob.html)
, that is if you specify a Mob in <entity\_uuid | player\_name>, they will not be used. The <continue\_after\_stop> option only supports entities which are a [Mobarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Mob.html)
, that is if you specify not a Mob in <entity\_uuid | player\_name>, it will not be used.

**Why some options have** **purple tag****? THESE OPTIONS CONTAIN EXPERIMENTAL FEATURES!** It means that <continue\_after\_stop> option is experimental fully, and <entity\_uuid | player\_name> option will be experimental if you specify entity which will not be a [Mobarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Mob.html)
.

**Who are not a** [**Mob**arrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Mob.html)
**s?** For example boat or you as a player - not a mobs, but zombie or pig - are a mobs.

**Why so many difficulties?** Server core internal functions do not implement half of the necessary functionality, so many features are implemented from zero by custom algorithms.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to force some entity or player to move somewhere until they are arrived there, all this with automatic best moving way finding (that is, path finding).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_destination: SET;%player%;world,-10442,64,-4294;true;true;true;1.0' # Force the current player to moving to the specified location with locked view direction, moving him if flying too and with increased speed to 1.0

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**This action is only for Paper and above!**

[Previouschange\_visibilitychevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_visibility)
[Nextchange\_experiencechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_experience)

Last updated 8 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_gliding | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding#meaning)

Allows you to change the gliding state of the entities when they are wearing elytra. However this will work even if an Elytra is not equipped, but will be reverted by the server immediately after unless an event-cancelling mechanism is put in place.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding#format)

Copy

    - 'change_gliding: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<true|false>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the gliding state for; (MANDATORY)

<true|false> – whether to disable or enable the gliding state. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding#targets)

*   [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
    ;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to forcely disable players gliding state when that are entering to the pvp mode.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_gliding#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_gliding: %player%;false' # Disable the gliding state of the current player

# change_name | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name#meaning)

Allows you to change the custom name of the entities, that is, the name which will be above their heads.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name#format)

Copy

    - 'change_name: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<action>;<name>;(optional) <visible (true|false)>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the name for; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be SET or RESET; (MANDATORY)

<name> – the new name to change the old name to (you can specify the empty name to change the only visibility in the "visible" option); (MANDATORY)

<visible> – the visibility state of the name, that is, only showing it while pointing to the target or always. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name#targets)

*   Entities;
    
*   [Nameablesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/Nameable.html)
    ;
    
*   Players (this is possible, but players are not affected by custom names for real).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name#where-is-useful)

For example if you want to make a bit more interesting your mobs and turn them into a little bit of customization changed the name.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_name: 805d4f5d-72cf-4e3d-80bc-b567da898786;SET;§cKiller;true' # Set the "§cKiller" name to some entity with constant visibility

* * *

[Previouschange\_movementchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement)
[Nextchange\_targetchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_target)

# manage_recipe | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe#meaning)

Allows you to give and take away discovered recipes from the players, that is, for example, you can force the player to forget how to craft the stone sword in the recipes book and so on.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe#format)

Copy

    - 'manage_recipe: <player>;<recipe_id>;<namespace>;<action>'

<player> – the player to change the discovery recipe for; (MANDATORY)

<recipe\_id> – the recipe to change (the recipes are the item names, for example: "stone\_sword"); (MANDATORY)

<namespace> – the namespace of the recipe, can be “Minecraft” (built-in minecraft crafts) and any other plugins or your own made-up namespaces (but third-party recipes will not be changed visually in the recipes book etc); (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be discover or forget. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

If you will chose "forget" action you still will be able to craft the items, the only changes will be that this recipe will not be in the recipes book now and if you "discover" it again then in the top-right minecraft corner you will see the appropriate message.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to troll somehow your players or make some kind of "achievements", for example, where players need to move up the "recipes-ladder" to more and more items.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe#examples)

Copy

    - 'manage_recipe: %player%;stone_sword;Minecraft;forget' # Forget the recipe of the stone sword for the current player

* * *

[Previouschange\_itemchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
[Nextchange\_flychevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fly)

# change_fly | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fly#meaning)

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fly#format)

Copy

    - 'change_fly: <player_name>;<action>;<true|false>'

<player\_name> – the player to change the fly; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be CURRENT or GLOBAL (the "CURRENT" action is responsible for the current flight state and the "GLOBAL" action is responsible for the permission to fly in general and is also setting current flight state); (MANDATORY)

<true|false> – whether to disable or enable the fly. (MANDATORY)

    - 'change_fly: %player%;CURRENT;true' # Enable the fly for the current player
