# Placeholder for entities in radius | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#meaning)

Allows you to get entities in radius by specified coordinates, both the fact of existence and number, and complete lists and values in these lists by index.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#format)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#check-presence-of-entities)

Check presence of entities:

Copy

    %CEP_entitiesInRadius_<world>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<radius>_<include (true|false)>_(optional) <filter1>,<filter2>,<filterN>% # Check if the entities exist at the location in the specified radius, will return "true" or "false"

<world>\_<x>\_<y>\_<z> – the central location to check the entities; (MANDATORY)

<radius> – the radius to check; (MANDATORY)

<include> – if current player exists, you can include it to the list or not; (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be mobs, players, items, vehicles, projectiles, hanging, falling, tnt or just entity types (you can also specify "!" before any types to exclude them from the list) (you can skip filters to get all entities, **but the last underscore should be in any case!**). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#get-count-of-entities)

Get count of entities:

Copy

    %CEP_entitiesCountInRadius_<world>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<radius>_<include (true|false)>_(optional) <filter1>,<filter2>,<filterN>% # Check the amount of the entities at the location in the specified radius, will return the amount

<world>\_<x>\_<y>\_<z> – the central location to check the entities; (MANDATORY)

<radius> – the radius to check; (MANDATORY)

<include> – if current player exists, you can include it to the list or not; (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be mobs, players, items, vehicles, projectiles, hanging, falling, tnt or just entity types (you can also specify ! before any types to exclude them from the list) (you can skip filters to get all entities). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#get-list-of-entities)

Get list of entities:

Copy

    %CEP_entitiesListInRadius_<world>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<radius>_<output>_<include (true|false)>_(optional) <filter1>,<filter2>,<filterN>% # Check the list of the entities at the location in the specified radius, will return the list of entities with data from the specified output

<world>\_<x>\_<y>\_<z> – the central location to check the entities; (MANDATORY)

<radius> – the radius to check; (MANDATORY)

<output> – the output to return, may be uuid, type, enum, name, coords or type,type ("type,type" is useful to get exactly the block type, and not the entity, for example, for “falling” filter); (MANDATORY)

<include> – if current player exists, you can include it to the list or not; (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be mobs, players, items, vehicles, projectiles, hanging, falling, tnt or just entity types (you can also specify ! before any types to exclude them from the list) (you can skip filters to get all entities). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#get-entity-at-index-in-list-of-entities)

Get entity at index in list of entities:

Copy

    %CEP_entityAtIndexInRadius_<world>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<radius>_<index_in_list>_<output>_<include (true|false)>_(optional) <filter1>,<filter2>,<filterN>% # Check the list of the entities at the location in the specified radius, will return the entity at the specified index in this list with data from the specified output

<world>\_<x>\_<y>\_<z> – the central location to check the entities; (MANDATORY)

<radius> – the radius to check; (MANDATORY)

<index\_in\_list> – the index in the list to return the entity; (MANDATORY)

<output> – the output to return, may be uuid, type, enum, name, coords or type,type ("type,type" is useful to get exactly the block type, and not the entity, for example, for “falling” filter); (MANDATORY)

<include> – if current player exists, you can include it to the list or not; (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be mobs, players, items, vehicles, projectiles, hanging, falling, tnt or just entity types (you can also specify ! before any types to exclude them from the list) (you can skip filters to get all entities). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**\-**" symbol instead of underscores in <filters>!

circle-info

Hanging - is a glowing frame, a regular frame, a tethered leash or a painting, check “All Known Subinterfaces” [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Hanging.html)
. Falling - is all falling blocks, such as sand or gravel when they fall, for this filter it is also useful “type,type” output option to get exactly the block type, and not the entity.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#targets)

*   Any entities.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to get entities in a radius at certain coordinates, find out if a certain entity is there and perform certain actions, like removing that entity via the [change\_entities](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_entities)
 action, modifying it via the [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action or in case of vehicles set the passenger of the found vehicle via [change\_passenger](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_passenger)
 action. To process a list from this placeholder, the [array](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)
 placeholder is very useful.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-entities-in-radius#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_entitiesListInRadius_{player_world}_{player_x}_{player_y}_{player_z}_10_uuid_false_players,mobs,!CREEPER% # Get the list of the uuids of entities at the player coordinates in 10 blocks radius including players and any living entities, excluding the current player and creepers

Copy

    %CEP_entityAtIndexInRadius_{player_world}_{player_x}_{player_y}_{player_z}_5_2_coords_false_vehicles% # Get the location of the third vehicle (at the second index, but counting from 0) in the list of entities at the player coordinates in 5 blocks radius  

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for biome by coordinateschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-biome-by-coordinates)
[NextPlaceholder for processing arrayschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays)

Last updated 8 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for different entity information | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information#meaning)

Allows you to get many different information of the entities, like health, air, location, passengers etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information#format)

Copy

    %CEP_entity_<action>_<separator>_(optional) <entity_uuid|player_name>%

<action> – may be type, name, enum, maxAir, currentAir, walkSpeed, flySpeed, hasAI, tags, ticksLived, isGliding, isBlocking, isHandRaised, currentHealth, maxHealth, isSwimming, isSitting, isInWater, isInLava, isFrozen, isInvisible, isInvulnerable, isOnFire:<real | visual>, fireTicks, location:<(optional, in any order) world,x,y,z,yaw,pitch>, openInventory, openInventorySize, inventory, inventorySize, passengers:<uuid | type | enum | name | coords>, target:<uuid | type | enum | name | coords>, canSee:<entity\_uuid | player\_name>, hasPath, path:<allPoints | lastPoint>, expPercent, targetBlock:<type | location | face>:<(may be empty) skipBlocks (throught comma in capital letters and with "-" instead of "\_")>:<(may be empty, default - 50) distance>:<(may be empty, default - ALWAYS) fluidMode (see possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/FluidCollisionMode.html)
, also use "-" instead of "\_")>, targetEntity:<type | location | face | uuid | enum | name>:<(may be empty, default - 50) distance>:<(may be empty, default - 0.5) raySize>, face, velocity:<x | y | z | xz | general>, color, pose (see available poses [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Pose.html)
), spawnReason, workBlock:<type | loc (optional "loc:<world,x,y,z (through comma, in any order and presence)>")>; (MANDATORY)

<separator> – the separator to separate the elements in different cases, it is needed when more than one element is outputting, for example in "location" (note that the in actions like "passengers" with "coords" output type, that is with several different nesting levels of elements, the separator will be applied only to the highest nesting level, for example: "world;x;y;z<separator>world;x;y;z", that is ";" or other internal separators will not be changed); (MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the UUID of an entity or the nickname of a player to get the information (you can skip it to use the current player). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-info

The "tags" <action> is ScoreboardTags, the "openInventory" and "openInventorySize" is the type or size of the open inventory of the player, the "inventory" and "inventorySize" is the type or size of the current inventory of the entity.

The "passengers" is the current passengers of the entity, "isBlocking" is for shields, "isHandRaised" is almost the same as "isBlocking", but activates instantly (while "isBlocking" activates after some delay), "target" is for an entity to which the specified entity is currently targeting.

The "canSee" outputs whether the player can see the entity or not (not potion effects, but hiding for example through the [change\_visibility](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_visibility)
 action, and note that the before 1.18 version you can check only visibility of the player, not entities).

The "hasPath" outputs whether the entity has the path for moving currently (everytime entity moves it has the path, but only [Mobarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Mob.html)
 entities (that is, entities like zombies, pigs and so on), otherwise you need to use for example [change\_destination](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_destination)
 to change the entity path), "path" outputs all coordinate points of the current path or the last point depending on the argument.

The "expPercent" outputs percentage of the player experience bar fullness.

The "targetBlock" outputs the block on which entity is looking, you can specify what to output in <output> option: type of the block, its location or facing (facing in case of blocks like doors, torches etc, see all types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/data/Directional.html)
); which blocks should be skipped for calculations in <skipBlocks> option, for example, if entity is targeting to the stone, it is possible to specify the "STONE" to skip it, **but do not forget to skip the AIR too, otherwise you will always get the block at the entity's head** (almost always AIR, only when you will be in some passable blocks like COBWEB or WATER it will return them); distance of the calculations in <distance> option and fluid collision mode in the <fluidMode> option (see all possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/FluidCollisionMode.html)
), fluid collision mode means whether the calculations will consider fluids or not (and some other special cases which you can see by the values link). **Note that when <skipBlocks> option is specified, <fluidMode> option is not counted!**

The "targetEntity" output the entity on which entity is looking, you can specify what to output in <output> option, desired distance in the <distance> option and how wide will be ray which touches the entities in the <raySize> option (0.4 is enough for the best accuracy, but you can specify for example 2 or even 3 and entities will expand their bounding boxes while doing calculations so that you will be able to catch entity even do not looking on it).

The "face" is for entity facing, for example NORTH or WEST and so on.

The "velocity" is the current velocity of the entity, you can specify which velocity you want to check, for example "general" for all three X, Y and Z dimensions, "xz" only for horizontal velocity, "Y" only for vertical velocity and so on.

The "color" outputs the color of the entity, for example sheeps or shulkers.

The "workBlock" outputs villagers working block type or location. **Only for Paper 1.20.5+!**

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information#targets)

*   Different entities (depends on the chosen action);
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to get different information about entities while implementing different systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_entity_currentAir_,_{player}% # Get the remaining air of the current player

Copy

    %CEP_entity_location:world,y_,_8977317d-0f8d-4aa7-9045-8ad7da785289% # Get the world and the Y coordinate of the specified entity separating by comma

Copy

    %CEP_entity_openInventory_,% # Get the open inventory type of the current player

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for custom datachevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data)
[NextPlaceholder for different block informationchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information)

# Installation or updation | CE AAPP

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#installation)

Installation:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#main-plugin)

Main plugin

Install the `TriggerReactor` plugin [**here**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/TriggerReactor/TriggerReactor/releases/download/3.5.0.6-Beta/TriggerReactor-bukkit-latest-3.5.0.6-Beta.jar)
;

triangle-exclamation

**DO NOT PAY ATTENTION ON THE TEXT BELOW IF YOU ARE A REGULAR USER WHICH DOES NOT ENCOUNTER ANY PROBLEMS.**

**Only for those who know what they are doing!** Use [this versionarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/TriggerReactor/releases/download/MythicDungeonsCompatibility/TriggerReactor-bukkit-latest-3.5.0.6-Beta.jar)
 to fix the Paper incorrect commands bug and compatibility with MythicDungeons (**this is EXPERIMENTAL version, please report all bugs**).

2

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#dependency-plugin)

Dependency plugin

Install the `TriggerReactor` dependency [**here**arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/jshader.93342/download?version=406835)
**;**

3

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#downloading-the-addon)

Downloading the addon

Download the newest version [**here**arrow-up-right](https://akcel.fun/ce-aapp)
 OR download all source content as archive on [**GitHub**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP)
;

4

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#setting-the-addon)

Setting the addon

Unpack the contents of the archive into the plugins folder (as a result, the **plugins folder** should contain the `TriggerReactor` folder with all its contents);

5

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#restarting)

Restarting

Restart the server;

6

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#final-checking)

Final checking

Make sure that everything is installed without errors: in the console you should see messages from `ConditionalEvents` and `PlaceholderAPI` about **successful registration** of new `actions` and new `expansion` respectively.

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#updation)

Updation:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#downloading-the-addon-1)

Downloading the addon

Download the newest version [**here**arrow-up-right](https://akcel.fun/ce-aapp)
 OR download all source content as archive on [**GitHub**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP)
;

2

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#deleting)

Deleting

Delete your previous `TriggerReactor` folder;

3

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#setting-the-addon-1)

Setting the addon

Unpack the contents of the archive into the plugins folder (as a result, the **plugins folder** should contain the `TriggerReactor` folder with all its contents);

4

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#restarting-1)

Restarting

Restart the server;

5

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation#final-checking-1)

Final checking

Make sure that everything is installed without errors: in the console you should see messages from `ConditionalEvents` and `PlaceholderAPI` about **successful registration** of new `actions` and new `expansion` respectively.

# Placeholder for custom moon phases | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#meaning)

Allows you to get custom moon phases in the night, for example when moon is on the top, it will be "FULL MOON".

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#format)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_<customState (true|false)>:(semi-optional) <customOutputs>_<world>%

<customState> – the state whether to get the number of the phase (**from 0 to 7**) or its appropriate name; (MANDATORY)

<customOutputs> – the custom output settings, that is how current output will be changed, **you can combine them via comma** (**use only in "true" case of the "customState" option**); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#the-customoutputs-possible-settings-by-default-english-words-with-spaces)

The "customOutputs" possible settings (by default - English words with spaces):

Us

Dh

Lc

Uc

FUc

ES

RU

EN

Replace spaces between words with underscores

Replace spaces between words with dashes

Lowercase all words

Uppercase all words

Uppecrase only first letter of each word

Spanish words

Russian words

English words

<world> – the world from which get the moon. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Note that the language custom output will override all already applied outputs, if specified at the end, **use language custom outputs at the start**!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#targets)

*   Worlds.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#where-is-useful)

It can be useful, for example, to add some more realism to the game, or implement some of your "role-playing" features.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_true:ES,Us,FUc_world% # Get the custom named moon phase in the world "world", in Spanish, underscoring spaces between words and uppercase only first letter of each word, for example "Luna_Creciente"

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_false_test_world% # Get the moon phase in the world "test_world", in number, for example 5

[PreviousPlaceholder for custom player listschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)
[NextModifying the addonchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/modifying-the-addon)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Placeholder for working with MySQL | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#meaning)

Allows you to work with MySQL and other external databases, using the JDBC link for the connection and performing different queries using PreparedStatement (default queries are suitable too).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#format)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_<connection_method>_(semi-mandatory) <jdbc_url>_(semi-mandatory) <sql_query>_(semi-mandatory) <param1>,<param2>,<paramN>%

<connection\_method> – the method to connect to the database through, may be SYNC or ASYNC, in case of "ASYNC" use format "ASYNC:<key>", you can just specify the "key" to get the data by it, or the full placeholder to save the data to this "key" (see more in the hint); (MANDATORY)

<jdbc\_url> – the JDBC link to connect to the database (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<sql\_query> – the query to the database (only obtaining the data) (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<params> – the substitutes for the "?" in the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query" (use it only in case if you are using the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query") (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores and "╵" symbol instead of percents everywhere! Only <connection\_method> is unaffectable, do not use underscores and percents in it at all.

circle-exclamation

"ASYNC" <connection\_method> allows you to return data asynchronously, you will get nothing from the common returning placeholder, it will just save the data to the specified key, only on the next time (for example, after one or more ticks delay), using the partial returning placeholder (that is, only <connection\_method>) you will get the data by the specified key. "SYNC" <connection\_method> works as usual, but it can load the server performance more!

circle-info

Not only PreparedStatements are available, default queries are suitable too.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#targets)

*   SQL queries.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to obtain data from the external databases in any way.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_SYNC_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Get three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" in a synchronous way

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Save three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" to the specified key in a asynchronous way
    # After one or more ticks delay
    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test% # Get the saved value by the specified key in previous placeholder

* * *

circle-info

Note that any external databases are suitable, not just MySQL.

[PreviousPlaceholder for different block informationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information)
[NextPlaceholder for checking structureschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_item | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#meaning)

Modifies items in players, entities and storages (chest, barrels etc) inventories, allows you to give, exchange, remove and customize different items in different ways, has very rich and useful functionality.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#format)

Copy

    - 'change_item: target:<entity_uuid|player_name|world,x,y,z>;<option>:<value>;<optionN>:<valueN>'

target:<entity\_uuid | player\_name | world,x,y,z> – the UUID of the target entity, the nickname of the target player or the target storage in which the items will be changed; (MANDATORY)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#options-any-order-but-at-least-one-should-be)

Options (any order, but at least one should be):

#### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#general-options)

General options:

source:<entity\_uuid | player\_name | world,x,y,z> – the source inventory from which the items will be taken; (OPTIONAL)

source\_slot:<slot> – the slot in the source inventory (only in case of specifying the "source" option); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

switch:<true | false> – whether to swap the items between the source and target inventories or just move the item from the source to the target (only in case of specifying the "source" option, can be skipped); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

action:<action> – may be set, remove, reset, increase, decrease, multiply or divide, it affects the "[item options](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#item-options-at-least-one-should-be-in-case-of-specifying-the-action-option)
", that is, whether the options will be set, or removed, or reset etc, most options support "set", "remove" and "reset", and only "amount" and "durability" for now support "increase", "decrease", "multiply" and "divide", that is, numerical operations (can be skipped in case of not specifying any "item options", and specifying for example only the "source" option); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

slot:<slot> | material:<material> – the slot or the material in the target inventory to change, can be many via "," (should be at least one of them); (MANDATORY)

counts:<counts> – indicates how many items will be changed; (OPTIONAL)

order:<order> – to specify the order of the "source", "slot" and "material" parameters execution through the comma and many other properties described below, in general this option means in which order, which options and how many times will be executed, that is, you can exclude some options, duplicate them several times etc, also you can configure the different options as you want; (OPTIONAL)

overrideOrderCountsOverGlobalCounts:<true | false> – if you want that "order" option local "counts" properties, if specified, to take precedence over the global "counts" option. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#the-general-format-of-the-less-than-order-greater-than-option)

The general format of the <order> option:

#### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#the-order-sub-options-format-it-is-optional-the-default-order-is-source-slot-material)

The order sub-options format (it is optional, the default order is "source,slot,material"):

> order:slot,material,source (for example) – execute first all modifiers under the "slot" option, then under the "material", and then under the "source" (it can be useful for example if you need firstly to change the items and then swap them with source, and not firstly swap and then change, of course in case of enabled "switch" option);
> 
> order:slot,source (for example) – execute first all modifiers under the "slot" option, then under the "source", and skip the "material" at all.

#### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#the-properties-format-they-are-also-optional)

The properties format (they are also optional):

> order:slot{<property1>=<value1>\`<propertyN>=<valueN>},material{<property1>=<value1>\`<propertyN>=<valueN>},source{<property1>=<value1>\`<propertyN>=<valueN>} (for example)

#### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#the-source-order-format-it-is-also-optional-the-default-order-is-slot-material)

The "source" order format (it is also optional, the default order is "slot\`material"):

> order:slot,material,source(material\`slot) (for example) – first change all materials to the source item, then all slots;
> 
> order:slot,material,source(material) (for example) – just change all materials to the source item, and skip the "slot" at all;

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#table-of-available-less-than-order-greater-than-option-properties)

Table of available <order> option properties:

Property

Objects

Values

Explanation

useSourceMaterialIfFurther

material

true / false

If "material" stands after "source" in order, whether to take the new material that came from source or not.

applyOpenedToSourceMaterial

material

ifExists / anyway

If the useSourceMaterialIfFurther property is specified to "true", whether to apply this material also to the player's open inventory or not. "ifExists" will consider the current value of the "material" option and will be applied only if "OPENED|<material>" exists there, and "anyway" will be applied in any way.

materialAdd | materialOverride

slotAdd | slotOverride

material and slot

The list through the "~"

It will add or override (you can and override and add) the current materials or slots from the "material" or "slot" option. You can use "CURSOR", "OPENED" etc as well.

counts

material, slot, source

Any number above 0

You can specify how many items will be changed for the each sub-option.

material.counts | slot.counts

source

Any number above 0

You can specify the personal counts for "material" and "slot" in "source", and not only general "counts" in the source.

useNewMaterialIfFurther

source

true / false

The same as useSourceMaterialIfFurther property, but vice versa, if "source" stands after the "material" or "slot" in order, whether to take the new material to which item changed or not (note that by changing the source only by slots and not materials, you will not change anything by this option).

applyOpenedToNewMaterial

source

ifExists / anyway

The same as applyOpenedToSourceMaterial property, but vice versa, if the useNewMaterialIfFurther property is specified to "true", whether to apply this material also to the player's open inventory or not. "ifExists" will consider the current value of the "material" option and will be applied only if "OPENED|<material>" exists there, and "anyway" will be applied in any way.

overridePartialCountsOverGeneralCounts

source

true / false

Whether to override material.counts and slot.counts properties with default source counts or not.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#item-options-at-least-one-should-be-in-case-of-specifying-the-action-option)

Item options (at least one should be in case of specifying the "action" option):

newMaterial:<new\_material> – the new material of the item (can change items from the air and to the air as well); (OPTIONAL)

durability:<durability> – the new durability of the item; (OPTIONAL)

name:<name> – the new name of the item; (OPTIONAL)

lore:<lore> – the new lore of the item (in case of "set" action "line1|line2|line3" or in case of "remove" action just numbers separated by commas, like "1,4,7"); (OPTIONAL)

enchantments:<enchantments> – the new enchantments of the item in format "ENCHANTMENT\_1=LEVEL,ENCHANTMENT\_2=LEVEL" (note that the names of enchantments may be different on different versions); (OPTIONAL)

enchantmentsBook:<enchantments> – the new enchantments of the item as the enchanted book in format "ENCHANTMENT\_1=LEVEL,ENCHANTMENT\_2=LEVEL" (note that the names of enchantments may be different on different versions); (OPTIONAL)

flags:<flags> – the new flags of the item, see the available flags [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/ItemFlag.html)
 (note that the names and presence of flags may be different on different versions); (OPTIONAL)

amount:<amount> – the new amout of the item; (OPTIONAL)

customModelData:<customModelData> – the new custom model data of the item; (OPTIONAL)

dataContainer:<name>,<id>,<type>,<value> – the new PersistentDataContainer of the item (the "type" and "value" should be used only in case of "set" action, the "value" should be wrapped in \[ \] in case of array types in "type"), see the available types for "type" [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/persistence/PersistentDataType.html)
 (but not all types are supported yet), for example, the ExecutableItems plugin adds a PersistentDataContainer with <name> “executableitems”, <id> “ei-id” and <type> “STRING” to its items, this is what you specify when you create the item in the /ei create <id> command, carefully use only appropriate values for appropriate types, for example, integer - integer, string - string. Name and id of the dataContainer should not contain any capital letters!; (OPTIONAL)

maxStack:<maxStack> – the new maximum stack of the item, should be above 1 and below 99, but values above 64 will not be displayed visually, only when changing the <amount> option (only 1.20.5+); (OPTIONAL)

cooldown:<ticks> – the current cooldown to set to the item like ender pearles or shields, it will set the cooldown for the item once - when you uses this action. Setting cooldown by slots is only available on the 1.21.2+ versions, otherwise use setting by material. This option is available only for players; (OPTIONAL)

cooldownBasic:<seconds> – the basic cooldown to set to the item like ender pearles or shields (supports float values), it will activates every time when player uses an item, not just once when you uses this action, like in the <cooldown>. Setting basic cooldown is only available on the 1.21.3+ versions. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

The <slot>, <source\_slot> and <material> options support "OPENED|<option>" to obtain the items in the player’s open inventory and "EC|<option>" to obtain the items in the player’s enderchest. Also the <slot> and <material> options support specifying many objects via "," (<source\_slot> does not support). The <slot> and <source\_slot> option also support "CURSOR" slot to obtain the item at the player's cursor and different named slots such as "HAND", see all possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/EquipmentSlot.html)
.

circle-exclamation

Even in case of <action> options "remove" or "reset", you need to specify the values of the options you want to remove, these values can be any, but not empty (for example just "name:0").

circle-exclamation

The <cooldown> option should be specified in ticks, and <cooldownBasic> in seconds, but you can also use float values in the <cooldownBasic>, like 0.05 seconds will be 1 tick.

The <cooldownBasic> set to the item will exclude this item from the common "material" list if you will want to specify <cooldown> by material, so you will need or reset the <cooldownBasic> or use setting <cooldown> by slot if your version allows it.

You can use <cooldown> only with players and <cooldownBasic> with any available targets.

The <cooldown> set by material will override the <cooldown> set by slot in the same action.

triangle-exclamation

If something is not working as you intended, most likely you are just doing something wrong!

circle-info

The amount of the options is not limited, you can specify as many you want combining one options with another.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#targets)

*   Entities ([InventoryHoldersarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/InventoryHolder.html)
     or [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
    );
    
*   Players;
    
*   Storages ([InventoryHoldersarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/InventoryHolder.html)
    ).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in any cases where you need to modify the storages, entities or player inventories and items in them in any ways, for example in some technical systems or mini-games.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_item: target:%player%;slot:HEAD,CHEST,LEGS,FEET;action:set;durability:150' # Just change the items durability on the armor slots of the current player

Copy

    - 'change_item: target:%player%;material:OPENED|STONE;action:set;newMaterial:COBBLESTONE;counts:10' # Change all stones to the cobblestones in the open inventory of the current player and limit it to the 10 changings

Copy

    - 'change_item: target:%player%;source:d3cb4dcc-95c1-4214-8296-db81b7a6eb2a;source_slot:HAND;material:DIAMOND_PICKAXE,NETHERITE_AXE;slot:10,15,HAND;action:set;newMaterial:DIAMOND_SWORD;enchantments:DAMAGE_ALL=1;switch:true;order:source(material`slot),material{useSourceMaterialIfFurther=true}' # First swap all diamond pickaxes and netherite axes in the current player inventory with some item from the source slot "HAND" from some entity, then swap "10", "15" and "HAND" slots in the current player inventory with the "HAND" slot from the source entity (there already will be netherite axe as last material), and then apply all item modifiers ("newMaterial" and "enchantments") to the material from the source, that is, netherite axes

* * *

[Previouschange\_targetchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_target)
[Nextmanage\_recipechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe)

# change_oraxen_block | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ORAXEN**arrow-up-right](https://oraxen.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#meaning)

Allows you to place and remove blocks from the Oraxen plugin at a specified location, since there are not any commands in Oraxen for that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: <mode>;<world,x,y,z>;<block_id|forceDrop (true|false)>;(semi-optional) <player>'

<mode> – may be SET or REMOVE, the "SET" will place the block, and the "REMOVE" will break the block if it will be an Oraxen block; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location to change the block; (MANDATORY)

<block\_id | forceDrop> – the block id to place (only in case of "SET" mode) or the forceDrop state, that is, whether to force the block to drop, even if player is null or in creative mode (only in case of "REMOVE" mode). (MANDATORY)

<player> – the player who caused the block to break (only in case of "REMOVE" mode, but can be skipped). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#targets)

*   Oraxen blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to place or break some blocks from Oraxen.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block#examples)

* * *

[Previouschange\_balancechevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance)
[Nextchange\_items\_adder\_blockchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: SET;world,14,64,123;customblocks:workbench' # Place the some custom workbench at the specified location

Copy

    - 'change_oraxen_block: REMOVE;world,14,64,123;true;%player%' # Break the some custom block at the specified location with a forced drop and as if said player had done it

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for processing arrays | CE AAPP v3.5 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#meaning)

Allows you to process arrays (strings separated by separators) in any ways, simply and quickly. Like "1,2,3,4,5" - the array separated by comma, and you can get some element by index in it, remove it and so on.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#format)

Copy

    %CEP_array_<separator>_<operation>_<array>_(semi-mandatory) <start_index>_(semi-mandatory) <end_index>_(semi-mandatory) <value>_(semi-mandatory) <new_value>%

<separator> – the separator which is separating data in the string (the more often separators are "," and ";"); (MANDATORY)

<operation> – may be GET, GET-PART, GET-BY-INDEX, GET-COUNT-BY-VALUE, GET-INDEXES-BY-VALUE, GET-LENGTH, CHECK, ADD-BY-INDEX, SET-BY-INDEX, SET-BY-VALUE, SET-RANGE, REMOVE-BY-INDEX, REMOVE-BY-VALUE or REMOVE-RANGE; (MANDATORY)

<array> – the array itself (string separated by specified separator, it also supports underscores); (MANDATORY)

<start\_index> – the start index for the data (only in case of "GET-PART", "GET-BY-INDEX", "ADD-BY-INDEX", "SET-BY-INDEX", "SET-RANGE", "REMOVE-BY-INDEX" and "REMOVE-RANGE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<end\_index> – the end index for the data (only in case of "GET-PART", "SET-RANGE" and "REMOVE-RANGE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<value> – the value for the data (only in case of "GET-COUNT-BY-VALUE", "GET-INDEXES-BY-VALUE", "CHECK", "ADD-BY-INDEX", "SET-BY-INDEX", "SET-BY-VALUE", "SET-RANGE" and "REMOVE-BY-VALUE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<new\_value> – the new value for the data (only in case of "SET-BY-VALUE" action). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-check

In case of "**GET-COUNT-BY-VALUE**", "**GET-INDEXES-BY-VALUE**", "**CHECK**", "**SET-BY-VALUE**" and "**REMOVE-BY-VALUE**" operations you can use any **conditions** in "value" values the same as [herearrow-up-right](https://ajneb97.gitbook.io/conditionalevents/conditions#type-of-conditionals)
, you can also use "**AND**", "**OR**" and their combinations with brackets for priority defining!

See more in [examples](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#examples)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#table-of-required-array-parameters-for-different-operations-and-operations-meaning-checkmarks-are-wh)

Table of required array parameters for different operations and operations meaning (checkmarks are what must necessarily be used (or optional if specified)):

Operation

Meaning

<start\_index>

<end\_index>

<value>

<new\_value>

GET

Get the whole array back

GET-PART

Get the part of the array back

check

check

GET-BY-INDEX

Get the element by index in the array

check

GET-COUNT-BY-VALUE

Get the amount of elements in the array

check

GET-INDEXES-BY-VALUE

Get the elements indexes in the array

check

GET-LENGTH

Get the length of the array

CHECK

Check if the value exists in the array

check

ADD-BY-INDEX

Add the element to the array by index

check

check

SET-BY-INDEX

Set the element in the array by index

check

check

SET-BY-VALUE

Set the certain values in the array to the new values

check

check

SET-RANGE

Set the range in the array to the new values

check

check

check

REMOVE-BY-INDEX

Remove the element in the array by index

check

REMOVE-BY-VALUE

Remove the certain values in the array

check

REMOVE-RANGE

Remove the range in the array

check

check

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <value> and <new\_value>!

circle-exclamation

The counting in the array is starting from 0, consider it!

circle-exclamation

Options that are not needed for one <operation> or another should be completely skipped, and not just left empty!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#targets)

*   String separated by separators (arrays).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#where-is-useful)

For example, you have a list of players that you need to process somehow: create another list, considering certain conditions for each player, and so on. Of course, you will also need to make some script in ConditionalEvents, but with this placeholder its size and complexity will be 100 times less, no exaggeration.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_array_,_GET-BY-INDEX_test1,test2,1,2,test5_2% # Get the third (counting from 0) element of the specified array, that is, number "1"

Copy

    %CEP_array_,_REMOVE-BY-INDEX_test1,test2,1,2,test5_1% # Remove the second (counting from 0) element in the specified array, that is, "test2" value

Copy

    %CEP_array_,_SET-BY-VALUE_test1,test2,1,2,test5_contains 5 OR > 1_NEW% # Set the last two values to the "NEW" value because only they are accomplish the conditions

Copy

    %CEP_array_,_GET-INDEXES-BY-VALUE_test1,test2,1,2,test5,goodOP2_(startsWith test OR startsWith good) AND contains 2% # Get the first (counting from 0) and the last values because only they are accomplish the conditions

* * *

chevron-rightDifferent videos[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v3.5/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-processing-arrays#different-videos)

![Cover](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3292329496-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyGSBqQxnCZUDpr5hFv4d%252Fuploads%252FUGhI69wBEQpjbXeaqga4%252F%25D0%259F%25D1%2580%25D0%25B5%25D0%25B2%25D1%258C%25D1%258E.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D928b0575-82e9-472c-be7d-1cfc7604ae2a&width=490&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38431968&sv=2)

[Array Placeholder Tutorialarrow-up-right](https://youtu.be/oVnsmetYg_A?si=JQCJ_SE0kVGP3Zg3)

Author: Optifyne

# change_balance | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ESSENTIALSX**arrow-up-right](https://essentialsx.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#meaning)

Allows you to change the balance of EssentialsX players using subtraction, multiplication, division operations and so on. Offline players are also supported.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#format)

Copy

    - 'change_balance: <player|player_uuid>;<amount>;<operation>'

<player | player\_uuid> – the player to change the balance (may be offline as well, **better use UUIDs for offline players to avoid possibility of small lags**, **for UUIDs obtaining always without lags the uuidASYNC option from** [**entity**](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)
 **placeholders is useful**); (MANDATORY)

<amount> – the amount to change the balance; (MANDATORY)

<operation> – may be SET, ADD, REMOVE, MULTIPLY, DIVIDE or RESET. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to change a player's balance without using Essentials commands (to avoid displaying a feedback message in some cases and so on).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_balance#examples)

* * *

[PreviousPlugins actionschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions)
[Nextchange\_oraxen\_blockchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_balance: %player%;1000;SET' # Set the specified player's current balance to 1000

Copy

    - 'change_balance: %player%;3;DIVIDE' # Divide the specified player's current balance by 3

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_projectile | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**THIS ACTION ONLY WORKS WHEN USING** [**EntityShootBowEvent**arrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/event/entity/EntityShootBowEvent.html)
 **EVENT.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#meaning)

Allows you to change the projectile when shooting from a bow, crossbow, etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#format)

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: <projectile_type|projectile_uuid>'

<projectile\_type | projectile\_uuid> – the UUID of already existed projectile or the type of some new projectile, like Snowball or Arrow (you can find valid projectile types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Projectile.html)
, but not all of them will work). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#targets)

*   Any [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
     which firing the event by shooting from the bow.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create an apocalypse by making everyone shoot fireballs, or, conversely, create a prank by turning projectiles into llama spit.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions/change_projectile#examples)

* * *

circle-info

Please note that by specifying the UUID of any lying item, the projectile will in any case be changed to an dirt item.

[PreviousEvents actionschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions)
[NextIndependent actionschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: Fireball' # Change the projectile to a fireball

Copy

    - 'change_projectile: d32893e0-c22b-41a6-8d74-ea785a1975ea' # Change the projectile to a some existing projectile (for example, Enderpearl)

# drop_items_adder_item | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ITEMSADDER**arrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#meaning)

Allows you to drop the items from the ItemsAdder plugin at a specified location not only with the /iadrop command in the ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#format)

Copy

    - 'drop_items_adder_item: <world,x,y,z>;<item_id>'

<world,x,y,z> – the location to drop the item; (MANDATORY)

<item\_id> – the item id to drop (in format namespace:id, check [itarrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.devs.beer/plugin-usage/beginners/configs-and-resourcepack#what-is-a-namespace)
 for more info). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#targets)

*   ItemsAdder items.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#where-is-useful)

For example, if you only need to use built-in actions and not third-party commands, then you could use this action to drop an item from the ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item#examples)

* * *

# change_spectating | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**PROTOCOLLIB**arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/protocollib.1997/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#meaning)

Allows you to change the spectation target of the specified player, leaving him on his real place, that is the player will spectate to the specified target like with the "/spectate" command or left-click in spectator gamemode, but the difference will be that you do not have to be in spectator gamemode and your in-game person will leave on his current place, while you will spectating.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#format)

Copy

    - 'change_spectating: <player>;<entity_uuid|player_name>'

<player> – the player for which change the spectation target; (MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the spectation target (you can use the same player to return his view). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to force some player to spectate to some entity simultaneously leaving him on his current place and leaving him exposed to any damage etc, like he is not spectating currently.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_spectating#examples)

* * *

[Previousshow\_end\_creditschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/show_end_credits)
[NextEvents actionschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/events-actions)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_spectating: %player%;c76bf00c-84f6-4556-99dc-eafec4ab847d' # Change the spectation target of the current player to some entity

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_items_adder_block | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ITEMSADDER**arrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#meaning)

Allows you to place and remove blocks from the ItemsAdder plugin at a specified location, since there are not any commands in ItemsAdder for that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: <mode>;<world,x,y,z>;(semi-mandatory) <block_id>'

<mode> – may be SET or REMOVE, the "SET" will place the block, and the "REMOVE" will break the block if it will be an ItemsAdder block; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location to change the block; (MANDATORY)

<block\_id> – the block id to place (only in case of "SET" mode, in format namespace:id, check [itarrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.devs.beer/plugin-usage/beginners/configs-and-resourcepack#what-is-a-namespace)
 for more info). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#targets)

*   ItemsAdder blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to place or break some blocks from ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#examples)

* * *

[Previouschange\_oraxen\_blockchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block)
[Nextdrop\_items\_adder\_itemchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: SET;world,14,64,123;customblocks:furnace' # Place the some custom furnace at the specified location

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: REMOVE;world,14,64,123' # Break the some custom block at the specified location

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Logical notations | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

*   (MANDATORY) – must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder;
    
*   (SEMI-MANDATORY) – must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, the current value does not need to be specified, but if it is specified in the required value, it is necessary);
    
*   (SEMI-OPTIONAL) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, it is not necessary to specify the current value, and if it is specified in the required value, it can be specified optionally);
    
*   (SEMI-OPTIONAL | SEMI-MANDATORY) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified to some value, or must necessarily be specified in the action/placeholder provided that some other option is specified to some another value (that is, if another option is specified in some wrong value or not specified at all depending on the requirements, it is not necessary to specify the current value, but if it is specified in the required value, it is necessary);
    
*   (OPTIONAL) – can optionally be specified in the action/placeholder.
    

circle-exclamation

The concepts used from action to action may vary depending on the implementation of the explanation of the format and principle of operation of the action.

[PreviousInstallation or updationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation)
[NextActionschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions)

# Starting information | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

👋 Hello, this **addon** adds a big pack of new **actions** and **placeholders** to `ConditionalEvents`, with it you have **full control** over entities, players, storages and many other useful features: everything that was previously possible only through vanilla commands or **not possible at all** in `ConditionalEvents`, is **now possible** directly in the built-in **actions** or **placeholders**.

The **main goal** of the addon is to provide as **much functionality** as possible in addition to the existing one, **quality** tries not to be inferior to **quantity**.

* * *

circle-check

**❗Join the original** [**ConditionalEvents Discord**arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/698332177137401987/1348313697436569733)
 **to the origin of this addon.**

triangle-exclamation

⚠️ Please report any problems or bugs you find, and suggest ideas for new features (to "[Issuesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Optifyne/CE-AAPP/issues)
" on GitHub, "[Discussionarrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/threads/conditionalevents-actions-and-placeholders-pack-ce-aapp.685662/)
" or [direct messagesarrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/conversations/)
 on Spigot or [direct messagesarrow-up-right](https://discordapp.com/users/440067456229179393)
 in Discord).

[PreviousLatest updateschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0)
[NextInstallation or updationchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/installation-or-updation)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for real nickname in Essentials based on custom nickname | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ESSENTIALSX**arrow-up-right](https://essentialsx.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#meaning)

Essentials has the /realname command to get a player's real nickname by customizing from the /nick command, but no placeholder. This placeholder allows you to get a player's real nickname by specifying their custom nickname from Essentials.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#format)

Copy

    %CEP_realname_(optional) <player>%

<player> – the player to check (you can skip it to use the current player). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to check and use real player nicknames by getting them through a placeholder, rather than just checking through a command with no further use possible.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#examples)

* * *

circle-info

Please note that the prefix specified in the nickname-prefix parameter in the config.yml file in the Essentials folder is also counted as part of the nickname.

[PreviousPlaceholder for LuckPerms permissions with contextschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts)
[NextPlaceholder for different information about EssentialsX warpschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    %CEP_realname_~SecretUser% # Get the real nickname of the player with the custom nickname ~SecretUser

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for checking last number value in LuckPerms's permission | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**LUCKPERMS**arrow-up-right](https://luckperms.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-last-number-value-in-luckpermss-permission#meaning)

Allows you to check the last number value in permission in LuckPerms plugin. For example, if permission is "customsystem.restriction.5", then the placeholder will return 5.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-last-number-value-in-luckpermss-permission#format)

Copy

    %CEP_permValue_<permission>_<player_name|player_uuid|group>%

<permission> – the starting permission part, for example if permission is "**customsystem.restriction.5**", then the starting part will be "**customsystem.restriction.**" (yes, exactly with dot!). (MANDATORY)

<player\_name | player\_uuid | group> – the UUID or the nickname of the online or offline player, **or the group in format "group-<group>"**. (MANDATORY)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**Be careful while specifying nicknames of offline players, this can cause a small lag! Better use UUIDs instead.**

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-last-number-value-in-luckpermss-permission#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-last-number-value-in-luckpermss-permission#where-is-useful)

For example, if you are making some system where you have certain restrictions based on permissions in one or another system parts, for example you want to make your own restrictions for WorldGuard regions, then you can give the permission to some player/group, for example, "worldguard.maxregions.5", then you can check when player creates a region his current regions amount in [Placeholder for checking regions amount of players](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players)
 placeholder and maximum regions amount in this placeholder, then perform different actions.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-last-number-value-in-luckpermss-permission#examples)

[PreviousPlaceholder for checking regions amount of playerschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players)
[NextIndependent placeholderschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders)

Last updated 4 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    %CEP_permValue_customsystem.turborestriction._group-vip% # Get the last number value of the "customsystem.turborestriction." permission of the "vip" group

# Placeholder for checking regions amount of players | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**WORLDGUARD**arrow-up-right](https://dev.bukkit.org/projects/worldguard)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players#meaning)

Allows you to check the amount of regions of some player in WorldGuard plugin, either in some world or globally.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players#format)

Copy

    %CEP_regions_<world>_<player_name|player_uuid>%

<world> – the world to get the amount from **or "global" to get the amount from all worlds in total** (**use "ᵕ" symbol instead of underscores in worlds names**); (MANDATORY)

<player\_name | player\_uuid> – the UUID or the nickname of the online or offline player. (MANDATORY)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**Be careful while specifying nicknames of offline players, this can cause a small lag! Better use UUIDs instead.**

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-regions-amount-of-players#where-is-useful)

Wherever you need to obtain information about how many regions some player has.

* * *

# change_items_adder_block | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ITEMSADDER**arrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.com/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#meaning)

Allows you to place and remove blocks from the ItemsAdder plugin at a specified location, since there are not any commands in ItemsAdder for that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#format)

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: <mode>;<world,x,y,z>;(semi-mandatory) <block_id>'

<mode> – may be SET or REMOVE, the "SET" will place the block, and the "REMOVE" will break the block if it will be an ItemsAdder block; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location to change the block; (MANDATORY)

<block\_id> – the block id to place (only in case of "SET" mode, in format namespace:id, check [itarrow-up-right](https://itemsadder.devs.beer/plugin-usage/beginners/configs-and-resourcepack#what-is-a-namespace)
 for more info). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#targets)

*   ItemsAdder blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to place or break some blocks from ItemsAdder.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_items_adder_block#examples)

* * *

[Previouschange\_oraxen\_blockchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/change_oraxen_block)
[Nextdrop\_items\_adder\_itemchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/plugins-actions/drop_items_adder_item)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: SET;world,14,64,123;customblocks:furnace' # Place the some custom furnace at the specified location

Copy

    - 'change_items_adder_block: REMOVE;world,14,64,123' # Break the some custom block at the specified location

sun-brightdesktopmoon
