# manage_mysql | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql#meaning)

Allows you to work with MySQL and other external databases, using the JDBC link for the connection and performing different queries using PreparedStatement (default queries are suitable too).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql#format)

Copy

    - 'manage_mysql: <jdbc_url>;<sql_query>;(semi-mandatory) <param1>,<param2>,<paramN>'

<jdbc\_url> – the JDBC link to connect to the database; (MANDATORY)

<sql\_query> – the query to the database (only modifying the data); (MANDATORY)

<params> – the substitutes for the "?" in the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query" (use it only in case if you are using the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query"). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-info

Not only PreparedStatements are available, default queries are suitable too.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql#targets)

*   SQL queries.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to modify data in the external databases in any way.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_mysql#examples)

Copy

    - 'manage_mysql: jdbc:mysql://u256340_PIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN%44ySggXPCF%2B56uFLpC39za%5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450_TESTDB;INSERT INTO Economy (Player, Target, Date, Action, Amount, NewBalance, Source) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);%player%,NULL,2025-05-17 20:30:00,ObtainingMoney,150.0,58259.0,API (Plugin)' # Insert new data to the Economy table

* * *

circle-info

Note that any external databases are suitable, not just MySQL.

[Nextchange\_hotbar\_slotchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_hotbar_slot)

# Placeholder for the highest block at a location | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#meaning)

Allows you to get the Y coordinate or type of the highest block at the specified location.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#format)

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_<player_name|entity_uuid|world,x,z>%

<player\_name | entity\_uuid | world,x,z> – the target on which location get the block (**you can specify ":type" at the end of any target to obtain the block type and not Y coordinate**). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to create some kind of random teleporting on your own, then you will need to get the highest block at your random chosen location to teleport the player there.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_8775c97f-3a4c-4906-ba63-80b950bc80c6% # Get the Y coordinate of the highest block at the specified entity location

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_world,242,3543:type% # Get the type of the highest block at the specified coordinates

# create_explosion | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#meaning)

Allows you to create the customizable explosions like spawning different TNTs or performing instant explosions.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#format)

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: <world>;<x>;<y>;<z>;<type>;<power>;(semi-mandatory) <delay>;(semi-mandatory) <set_fire (true|false)>;(semi-mandatory) <break_blocks (true|false)>;(semi-optional) <source_entity (entity_uuid|player_name)>'

<world>;<x>;<y>;<z> – the location to create the explosion; (MANDATORY)

<type> – may be TNT or EXPLOSION; (MANDATORY)

<power> – the power of the explosion (can be in float); (MANDATORY)

<delay> – the delay before the explosion in ticks (only in case of "TNT" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<set\_fire> – whether to make the blocks on fire after the explosion or not (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<break\_blocks> – whether to break the blocks after the explosion or not (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<source\_entity> – the entity which caused the explosion (only in case of "EXPLOSION" type, can be skipped). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#table-of-required-options-for-different-types-checkmarks-are-what-must-necessarily-be-used-or-option)

Table of required options for different types (checkmarks are what must necessarily be used (or optional if specified)):

TYPE

<world>;<x>;<y>;<z>

<power>

<delay>

<set\_fire>

<break\_blocks>

<source\_entity>

TNT

check

check

check

EXPLOSION

check

check

check

check

check

(optional)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Options that are not needed for one <type> or another should be completely skipped, and not just left empty.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#targets)

*   Locations.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to create some apocalypse and blowing everything up, or create pretty popular "tnt-sheep" which will be blowed after some time of living.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/create_explosion#examples)

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: world;52;64;634;TNT;10;100' # Spawn the tnt at the specified location with 10 explosive power and 100 ticks (5 seconds) delay before the explosion

Copy

    - 'create_explosion: world;52;64;634;EXPLOSION;10;true;true;%player%' # Create the explosion at the specified location with 10 explosive power, making the blocks on fire and breaking them, using the current player as the source of the explosion

# change_movement | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#meaning)

Allows you to change the different movement states of the entities (sneaking, sprinting etc).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#format)

Copy

    - 'change_movement: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<action>;<value>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the movement for; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be sprint, sneak, swim, sit or rotate; (MANDATORY)

<value> – the value to change the movement to ("true" or "false" in all actions except "rotate" action in which "yaw,pitch" as float values). (MANDATORY)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

Note that if the entity is affected by AI currently, the "rotate" option may not work pretty well, that is rotation may be overwrited by the path finding behavior almost immediately.

circle-exclamation

The "sneak" action is only visible to other players and not you, and the speed is not changing to slower. The "sprint" action is just the sprinting particles underfoot and sounds. The "swim" action does not change anything visually, it just changes the swimming state for a one tick. The "sit" action is only applicable to the sittable entities like dogs.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#targets)

*   [LivingEntitiesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/LivingEntity.html)
    ;
    
*   [Sittablesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Sittable.html)
    ;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to change different movement states of the entities.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_movement#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_movement: %player%;sneak;true' # Force the current player to sneak visually for other players

Copy

    - 'change_movement: 1548f301-d23d-4655-8e20-2e41905784dc;rotate;52,-27' # Force some entity to rotate in specified yaw and pitch

* * *

[Previouschange\_colorchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_color)
[Nextchange\_namechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_name)

# change_effect | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect#meaning)

Allows you to change the effects on the entities.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect#format)

Copy

    - 'change_effect: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<action>;<effect>;<strength>;<duration>;<show_particles (true|false)>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to change the effect; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be ADD, REMOVE or REMOVE\_ALL; (MANDATORY)

<effect> – the effect name (see effect types [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/potion/PotionEffectType.html)
, but note that they can change from version to version); (MANDATORY)

<strength> – the strength of the effect; (MANDATORY)

<duration> – the duration of the effect in ticks; (MANDATORY)

<show\_particles> – whether to show the particles of the effect or not. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect#targets)

    ;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to create some kind of "mob-arena" and put there different mobs with different possibilities (effects).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_effect#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_effect: d3cb4dcc-95c1-4214-8296-db81b7a6eb2a;ADD;INCREASE_DAMAGE;2;200;true' # Give the strength effect to some entity with 2 level and 200 ticks duration (10 seconds), hiding the particles

# Placeholder for real nickname in Essentials based on custom nickname | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ESSENTIALSX**arrow-up-right](https://essentialsx.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#meaning)

Essentials has the /realname command to get a player's real nickname by customizing from the /nick command, but no placeholder. This placeholder allows you to get a player's real nickname by specifying their custom nickname from Essentials.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#format)

Copy

    %CEP_realname_(optional) <player>%

<player> – the player to check (you can skip it to use the current player). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to check and use real player nicknames by getting them through a placeholder, rather than just checking through a command with no further use possible.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname#examples)

* * *

circle-info

Please note that the prefix specified in the nickname-prefix parameter in the config.yml file in the Essentials folder is also counted as part of the nickname.

[PreviousPlaceholder for LuckPerms permissions with contextschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts)
[NextPlaceholder for different information about EssentialsX warpschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    %CEP_realname_~SecretUser% # Get the real nickname of the player with the custom nickname ~SecretUser

# Placeholder for the highest block at a location | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#meaning)

Allows you to get the Y coordinate or type of the highest block at the specified location.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#format)

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_<player_name|entity_uuid|world,x,z>%

<player\_name | entity\_uuid | world,x,z> – the target on which location get the block (**you can specify ":type" at the end of any target to obtain the block type and not Y coordinate**). (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to create some kind of random teleporting on your own, then you will need to get the highest block at your random chosen location to teleport the player there.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_8775c97f-3a4c-4906-ba63-80b950bc80c6% # Get the Y coordinate of the highest block at the specified entity location

Copy

    %CEP_highestBlock_world,242,3543:type% # Get the type of the highest block at the specified coordinates

* * *

# change_craft | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_craft#meaning)

Allows you to create, modify, and delete different crafts in the workbench.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_craft#format)

Copy

    - 'change_craft: <recipe_id>;<action>;(semi-mandatory) <remove_namespace>;(semi-mandatory) <add_namespace>;(semi-mandatory) <craft_line_1>,<craft_line_2>,<craft_line_3>;(semi-mandatory) <result_item>;(semi-mandatory) <strict (true|false)>;(semi-mandatory) <ingredient_items>'

<recipe\_id> – the recipe/craft to change, the existing minecraft recipes are the item names (for example: stone\_sword) or it can be in another view in case of custom crafts; (MANDATORY)

<action> – may be ADD, REMOVE or CHANGE; (MANDATORY)

<remove\_namespace> – is needed in order to get a specific place where the craft needs to be removed from, for example, if craft has the same name in different plugins (specify "null" if you want to remove the recipe with default "TriggerReactor" plugin namespace), it can be "Minecraft" (built-in minecraft crafts), "All" (any suitable crafts in any namespaces), "CustomCrafting" (intended name of the plugin), “my\_test\_namespace” and any other plugins or your own made-up namespaces (this namespace should be used only with "REMOVE" or "CHANGE" actions, with "ADD" this value will be skipped, then you can leave it "null"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<add\_namespace> – is needed in order to get a specific place where the craft needs to be added, for example, if the craft has the same name in different plugins (specify "null" if you want to add new recipe with default "TriggerReactor" plugin namespace), it can be "Minecraft" (built-in minecraft crafts), "CustomCrafting" (intended name of the plugin), "my\_test\_namespace" and any other plugins or your own made-up namespaces (this namespace should be used only with "ADD" or "CHANGE" actions, with "REMOVE" this value will be skipped, then you can leave it "null"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<craft\_line\_1>,<craft\_line\_2>,<craft\_line\_3> – the craft "letters substitutes", is the same as craft lines in the workbench, i.e. “craft\_line\_1” is the first line and so on (for example: "AAA, BAB, ABA", for empty elements use spaces) (should be used only with "ADD" or "CHANGE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<result\_item> – the item in the craft result, it supports some meta in format amount:name:lore:enchantments:custom\_model\_data (unnecessary options can be skipped, for example: "DIAMOND\_SWORD:1:§cMega Sword::SHARPNESS=1") (should be used only with "ADD" or "CHANGE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<strict> – whether the ingredients in the crafting process must match the specified ingredients in all respects (such as lore, name etc), or whether only the material is sufficient (should be used only with "ADD" or "CHANGE" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<ingredient\_items> – the ingredients items, support some meta in format amount:name:lore:enchantments:custom\_model\_data as well (unnecessary options can be skipped), the correct general format: "<letter substitute>,<material>:<properties>" (for example: A,STICK:2:§cSuper-stick;B,DIAMOND:::::14) (should be used only with "ADD" or "CHANGE" actions). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Amount has no effect on ingredients.

circle-exclamation

Be careful, as the names of enchantments are different on different versions!

triangle-exclamation

Any namespace must contain either “Minecraft”, the name of some plugin, or your custom made-up name in the format \[a-z0-9.\_-\] (only small letters, numbers, dots, underscores and dashes), <remove\_namespace> can also contain “All” (as it is written above in the options explanation).

circle-info

The "lore" meta supports miltuply lore lines with "|" symbol.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_craft#targets)

*   Crafts/recipes.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_craft#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to make able to craft your custom items, or, vice versa, remove some existing items from the crafting possibility.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_craft#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_craft: custom_sword;ADD;null;custom_crafts; D , D , S ;DIAMOND_SWORD:2:§cSword "double profit!":DAMAGE_ALL=5;true;D,DIAMOND;S,STICK:::|§cSuper-stick' # Add a new craft with id "custom_sword" in "custom_crafts" custom namespace with the final item of a diamond sword named "§cSword "double profit!"", the ingredients of diamonds and a stick with lore "§cSuper-stick" on the second line, the arrangement of ingredients like a default diamond sword and strict matching of ingredients so that not only the material but also the lore etc are taken into account

Copy

    - 'change_craft: custom_sword;REMOVE;All' # Remove all crafts with "custom_sword" id in any namespaces or plugins

* * *

circle-info

It may be useful to use [manage\_recipe](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_recipe)
 action with this action to also remove the removed crafts from the recipes book etc.

[Previouschange\_flychevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_fly)
[Nextchange\_airchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_air)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# change_area | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_area#meaning)

Allows you to fill an area with blocks like in the WorldEdit plugin, using the different replacement modes and blocks ratios.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_area#format)

Copy

    - 'change_area: <world>;<x1>;<y1>;<z1>;<x2>;<y2>;<z2>;<block_to>;(optional) <mode>;(semi-mandatory) <block_from>'

<world>;<x1>;<y1>;<z1>;<x2>;<y2>;<z2> – the area to change; (MANDATORY)

<block\_to> – the block to which change the area; (MANDATORY)

<mode> – the mode in which way the blocks will be changed, may be replace, keep, outline or hollow; (OPTIONAL)

<block\_from> – the block from which to change the area (only in case of the "replace" mode). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-info

You can use many blocks via comma in <block\_to> and <block\_from> options. Also in <block\_to> option you can specify the percents like "55%STONE,10%DIAMOND\_BLOCK".

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_area#targets)

*   Any blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_area#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to change some area using blocks percents ratios and without using plugins like WorldEdit.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_area#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_area: %player_world%;%math_0:DOWN_{player_x}-2%;%player_y%;%math_0:DOWN_{player_z}-2%;%math_0:DOWN_{player_x}+2%;%math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-2%;%math_0:DOWN_{player_z}+2%;STONE,5%OAK_LOG;replace;AIR' # Replace all air to the mostly stone and a bit oak log blocks within the certain area at the current player location

* * *

[Previouschange\_healthchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_health)
[Nextchange\_statisticchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_statistic)

# Placeholder for different team information (/team) | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#meaning)

<action> – the information to get, may be name, size, members, color, prefix, suffix, visibility or collision. (MANDATORY)

# Independent placeholders | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

1.  [Placeholder for items](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
    ;

# Placeholder for checking whether the input can be an instance of a different objects | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects#meaning)

Allows you to check whether the input can be an instance of a different objects (for example, whether it is number, uuid etc).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects#format)

Copy

    %CEP_isObject_<data_type>_<input>%

<instance\_to\_compare> – the data type with which you need to compare your current object, may be number (aliases: num, n), integer (aliases: int, i), uuid (alias: u) and player (alias: p); (MANDATORY)

<input> – the input object. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

This placeholder will try to parse your object as specified <data\_type> and return you "true" or "false". **Note that the offline players nicknames while parsing with "player" <data\_type> may cause small delays, be careful with this!**

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects#targets)

*   Objects.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to check whether the input is a number or not (such variable also exists in ConditionalEvents, but only there, while this is global PlaceholderAPI placeholder).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_isObject_num_25d% # Will return "false" because "25d" is not a number

[PreviousPlaceholder for efficient counting specific blocks in chunkschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks)
[NextPlaceholder for replacing input through the RegExchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex)

# Placeholder for different team information (/team) | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#meaning)

Allows you to get different information about the vanilla teams, like size, members, prefix, different rules and so on.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#format)

Copy

    %CEP_team_<entity_uuid|player_name>_<action>%

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to get the information; (MANDATORY)

<action> – the information to get, may be name, size, members, color, prefix, suffix, visibility or collision. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#where-is-useful)

Wherever you would want to work with vanilla teams and get extensive information about them.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_team_{player}_size% # Get the size of the team of the current player

Copy

    %CEP_team_9926220f-475c-43b4-870a-024a1f6b7bed_name% # Get the name of the team of some entity

* * *

# Placeholder for checking structures | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#meaning)

Allows you to get a structure by specifying the location. Also you can check whether is the specified structure exists at the specified location or not.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#format)

Copy

    %CEP_structure_<action>_(semi-mandatory) <structure_type>_<x,y,z,world>%

<action> – the action to perform, may be get or check, "get" will return the structure type at the specified location, and "check" will return whether the structure type at the specified location equals to the specified <structure\_type> option (you can also use "<action>:unsafe:<(optional, by default 10) size>" to use the unsafe mode and its size, see more in the red hint); (MANDATORY)

<structure\_type> – the structure type to compare (use only in case of "check" <action>); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<x,y,z,world> – the location to check the structure. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "-" symbol instead of underscores in <structure\_type>!

triangle-exclamation

This placeholder sometimes may contain strange behavior of structure size/position definition (for example, with some swamp huts). In any "strange" cases (where the structure should be detected, but actually not being detected) you need to try to use "unsafe" option (unsafe because not precise), which will check blocks around in the specified radius (or in 10 blocks radius if radius is not specified), or check blocks around manually (but any way this offset only works inside the current chunk, and not outside).

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#targets)

*   Locations.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to check structures on a different locations.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_structure_get_-5307,72,-6940,world% # Get the sctructure at the specified location

Copy

    %CEP_structure_check:unsafe:15_SWAMP-HUT_1213,54,-440,test_world% # Check whether the sctructure at the specified location is swamp hut or not, also checking all blocks around in 15 radius

* * *

circle-exclamation

The unexplored/unloaded structures are not counted!

triangle-exclamation

This placeholder only works on 1.20.4+ versions!

[PreviousPlaceholder for working with MySQLchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql)
[NextPlaceholder for repeating the textchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text)

# Placeholder for efficient counting specific blocks in chunks | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks#meaning)

Allows you to check amount of specific blocks in chunks efficiently.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks#format)

Copy

    %CEP_countBlocks_<type>_<player_name|entity_uuid|world,x,y,z>%

<type> – the type of the block to count (**use "-" symbol instead of underscores**); (MANDATORY)

<player\_name | entity\_uuid | world,x,y,z> – the location of the chunk to check. (MANDATORY)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Location.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to count total amount of specific blocks in some chunk and prohibit to place more blocks with this type for players.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-efficient-counting-specific-blocks-in-chunks#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_countBlocks_CRAFTING-TABLE_world,44,0,345% # Get amount of the crafting tables in chunk by the specified location

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**This action is only for Paper 1.20.5 and above!**

# make_damage | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/make_damage#meaning)

Allows you to deal damage to the entities.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/make_damage#format)

Copy

    - 'make_damage: <entity_uuid|player_name>;<damage_amount>;(optional) <damager_uuid|player_name>'

<entity\_uuid | player\_name> – the target to deal the damage; (MANDATORY)

<damage\_amount> – the amount of the damage to deal; (MANDATORY)

<damager\_uuid | player\_name> – the damager which deal the damage. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/make_damage#targets)

*   [Damageablesarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/entity/Damageable.html)
    ;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/make_damage#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to damage the entity or player silently and with possibility to specify the damager without using the vanilla commands.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/make_damage#examples)

Copy

    - 'make_damage: %player%;10' # Damage 10 health to the current player

Copy

    - 'make_damage: d32893e0-c22b-41a6-8d74-ea785a1975ea;50;%player%' # Damage 50 health to some entity from the the current player

# Placeholder for working with MySQL | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#meaning)

Allows you to work with MySQL and other external databases, using the JDBC link for the connection and performing different queries using PreparedStatement (default queries are suitable too).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#format)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_<connection_method>_(semi-mandatory) <jdbc_url>_(semi-mandatory) <sql_query>_(semi-mandatory) <param1>,<param2>,<paramN>%

<connection\_method> – the method to connect to the database through, may be SYNC or ASYNC, in case of "ASYNC" use format "ASYNC:<key>", you can just specify the "key" to get the data by it, or the full placeholder to save the data to this "key" (see more in the hint); (MANDATORY)

<jdbc\_url> – the JDBC link to connect to the database (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<sql\_query> – the query to the database (only obtaining the data) (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<params> – the substitutes for the "?" in the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query" (use it only in case if you are using the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query") (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores and "╵" symbol instead of percents everywhere! Only <connection\_method> is unaffectable, do not use underscores and percents in it at all.

circle-exclamation

"ASYNC" <connection\_method> allows you to return data asynchronously, you will get "Loading..." text from the common returning placeholder, it will save the data to the specified key, and on the next time (for example, after one or more ticks delay), using the partial returning placeholder (that is, only <connection\_method>) you will get the data by the specified key. "SYNC" <connection\_method> works as usual, but it can load the server performance more!

circle-info

Not only PreparedStatements are available, default queries are suitable too.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#targets)

*   SQL queries.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to obtain data from the external databases in any way.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_SYNC_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Get three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" in a synchronous way

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Save three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" to the specified key in a asynchronous way
    # After one or more ticks delay
    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test% # Get the saved value by the specified key in previous placeholder

* * *

circle-info

Note that any external databases are suitable, not just MySQL.

# Placeholder for checking the distance between two points | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points#meaning)

Allows you to check the distance between two points, for example, between some player and some entity, or some player and some block, etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points#format)

Copy

    %CEP_distance_<player_name|entity_uuid|world,x,y,z>_<player_name|entity_uuid|world,x,y,z>%

<player\_name | entity\_uuid | world,x,y,z> – the points between which check the distance (**use "ᵕ" symbol instead of underscores everywhere**). (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Note that the worlds of the points should be the same!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Locations.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points#where-is-useful)

For example, to fastly and easily check the distance between some player and some entity/block and decide whether the player is nearby to it or not (such variable also exists in ConditionalEvents, but only there and only for players, while this is global PlaceholderAPI placeholder and for all types: players, entities and blocks).

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_distance_{player}_world,234,64,6344% # Get the distance between current player and specified location

[PreviousPlaceholder for replacing input through the multi replacementchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement)

# Placeholder for replacing input through the multi replacement | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement#meaning)

Allows you to replace input through the multi replacement in convenient and multifunctional way, that is, first value to one value, second value to another value, etc, like "a" to "b", "k" to "c" and so on, all in one placeholder.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement#format)

Copy

    %CEP_replaceMulti_<replacements>_<input>%

<replacements> – the replacements in format like "<from1>=<to1>:<from2>=<to2>:<fromN>=<toN>...", **you can use "\\:" and "\\=" to use colons and equal signs exactly as part as your replacements, and not part of format**; (MANDATORY)

<input> – the input for replacion. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

**You can use** **everywhere****:**

*   "ᵕ" symbol to replace to "\_" symbol
    
*   "╵" symbol to replace to "%" symbol
    
*   "<" symbol to replace to "{" symbol
    
*   ">" symbol to replace to "}" symbol
    

*   "\\ᵕ" symbol to replace to escaped "\\\_" symbol
    
*   "\\╵" symbol to replace to escaped "\\%" symbol
    
*   "\\<" symbol to replace to escaped "\\{" symbol
    
*   "\\>" symbol to replace to escaped "\\}" symbol
    

*   "\\\\ᵕ" symbol to replace to the original "ᵕ" symbol
    
*   "\\\\╵" symbol to replace to the original "╵" symbol
    
*   "\\\\<" symbol to replace to the original "<" symbol
    
*   "\\\\>" symbol to replace to the original ">" symbol
    

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement#targets)

*   Strings.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to replace one different values to another different values in some message with any difficilty level at the same time efficiently and easily.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_replaceMulti_abc=NEW:ohj=NEW2_ahs hwd oj ohj ab abc gerdg% # Replace all "abc" to "NEW" and all "ohj" to "NEW2"

Copy

    %CEP_replaceMulti_\:\=Hello=Bye:Hi=\=Goodbye\:_:=Hello hello hi Hi% # Replace all ":=Hello" to "Bye" and all "Hi" to "=Goodbye:"

[PreviousPlaceholder for replacing input through the RegExchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex)
[NextPlaceholder for checking the distance between two pointschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-the-distance-between-two-points)

# drop_current_item | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#meaning)

Allows you to drop the items from the player hand, and with new Paper versions it has even more functionality.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#format)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#spigot-and-below)

Spigot and below:

Copy

    - 'drop_current_item: <player>;<drop_all (true|false)>'

<player> – the player to drop the item from; (MANDATORY)

<drop\_all> – whether to drop all stack or only one item. (MANDATORY)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#paper-1.21.4-and-above)

Paper 1.21.4 and above:

Copy

    - 'drop_current_item: <player>;<drop_all|slot|material>;(semi-optional|semi-mandatory) <amount>;(semi-optional) <throwRandomly (true|false)>'

<player> – the player to drop the items from; (MANDATORY)

<drop\_all | slot | material> – whether to drop all stack or only one item ("true" or "false"), or slot from which drop the item, or material of the new item to drop (slots may be "HEAD", "CHEST" etc, see all possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/inventory/EquipmentSlot.html)
, or any possible number slots); (MANDATORY)

<amount> – the amount to drop (use optionally in case of specifying the slot or mandatory in case of specifying the material); (SEMI-OPTIONAL | SEMI-MANDATORY)

<throwRandomly> – whether to drop the items randomly or by the player view direction (will work only if "amount" is specified). (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#table-of-required-options-for-different-another-options-checkmarks-are-what-must-necessarily-be-used)

Table of required options for different another options (checkmarks are what must necessarily be used (or optional if specified)):

<drop\_all | slot | material>

<player>

<amount>

<throwRandomly>

drop\_all

check

slot

check

check

(optional)

check

(optional, but only if "amount" is specified)

material

check

check

check

(optional, but only if "amount" is specified)

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#targets)

*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to troll somehow your players or make some systems where certain items should be dropped from the player inventories.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/drop_current_item#examples)

Copy

    - 'drop_current_item: %player%;OFF_HAND' # In case of Paper 1.21.4+ drop the full stack of items from the off hand of the current player, or in case of Spigot and below drop the full stack of items from the main hand of the current player (because "OFF_HAND" it is like the "false")

Copy

    - 'drop_current_item: %player%;15;2;false' # In case of Paper 1.21.4+ drop the 2 items from the stack from the 15 slot of the current player, or in case of Spigot and below do nothing

Copy

    - 'drop_current_item: %player%;STONE;5;true' # In case of Paper 1.21.4+ drop the 5 stones from the current player (even if he did not have them), or in case of Spigot and below do nothing

* * *

# manage_cycle | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle#meaning)

Allows you to run and manage cycles for array processing effectively, that is without making cycles through call events in ConditionalEvents, which have certain resrtictions and performance issues, but with directly processing in code. This action will call the ConditionalEvents call event with transferred necessary variables. You will be able to perform any actions and check any conditions, as well as stop the specified cycle or change the array of the specified cycle.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle#format)

Copy

    - 'manage_cycle: <action>;<cycle_name>;<options (see below)>'

<action> – may be run, update or break, defines whether to run new cycle or update/break the current cycle; (MANDATORY)

<cycle\_name> – unique cycle name to store it, needed for "update" and "break" actions. (MANDATORY)

* * *

**Run** **action (for this action use options below):**

<from\_index> – the start index in the array, you can use "last" word for the last index in the array (**should be positive (zero is available), can be greater than <to\_index>, but then <step> should be negative**); (MANDATORY)

<to\_index> – the end index in the array, you can use "last" word for the last index in the array (**should be positive (zero is available**)); (MANDATORY)

<step> – step of processing (**regulary should be 1, but could be 2 and so on to "jump" through some elements etc, also can be negative, but can not be zero**); (MANDATORY)

<array\_separator> – separator symbol in the array (**can not be ";" symbol due to ConditionalEvents call events console command peculiarities**); (MANDATORY)

<array> – the array to process itself; (MANDATORY)

<call\_event> – the ConditionalEvents call event name to call, available variables are %v% (current value), %i% (current index), %s% (step), %c% (cycle name), %a% (current array), %l% (length of the current array), %f% ("+" if <step> is positive and "-" if <step> is negative), %end% ("true" or "false" whether this is the end of processing), %start% ("true" or "false" whether this is the start of processing) and %o% ("false" if the end of processing was due to the end of the array, "true" if the end of processing was due to out of bounds); (MANDATORY)

<player\_name> – to call the event for certain player. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

**Update** **action (for this action use options below):**

<changes> – the changes to perform on the array, the format is "<action>:<property1>:<property2>:<propertyN>...", actions may be ADD-BY-INDEX (alias: ABI) (properties: <index>:<value>), SET-BY-INDEX (alias: SBI) (properties: <index>:<value>), SET-BY-VALUE (alias: SBV) (properties: <old\_value>:<new\_value>), SET-RANGE (alias: SR) (properties: <start\_index>:<end\_index>:<value>), REMOVE-BY-INDEX (RBI) (properties: <index>) (**you can use "~" symbol in all "index" values for the last index in the array**). (MANDATORY)

* * *

**Break** **action (no options, just use the cycle name).**

* * *

triangle-exclamation

Indeces are always inclusive, it means, for example, that "from 0 to 5" will be "0, 1, 2, 3, 4 and 5"! The same for reverse: "from 10 to 4" will be "10, 9, 8, 7, 6, 5 and 4"!

circle-exclamation

Note! If you will specify too big <step>, you more often will face the situation where the last call event calling will return you the previous %v% (current value) and %i% (current index) variables, because "current\_index + current\_step" will go out of bounds of the array if the <step> is too big.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle#targets)

*   String separated by separators (arrays).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to process some array efficiently and fastly, performing some actions and checking some conditions on each value.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle#examples)

Copy

    - 'manage_cycle: run;cycle1;0;last;1;,;%CEP_customData_tempget_testArray%;testCall;%player%' # Run the cycle with "cycle1" name from start to end with "1" step, processing the array with "," separator from "testArray" variable from customData placeholder, and calling the "testCall" event for the current player

Copy

    - 'manage_cycle: update;cycle1;ABI:5:NEW' # Update the cycle with "cycle1" name by adding a new value "NEW" on the 5 index

Copy

    - 'manage_cycle: break;cycle1' # Break the cycle with "cycle1" name

* * *

[Previouschange\_hotbar\_slotchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_hotbar_slot)
[Nextchange\_spawnerchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Placeholder for repeating the text | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#meaning)

Allows you to repeat the text as many times as you will specify.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#format)

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_<text>_<amount>%

<text> – the text to repeat; (MANDATORY)

<amount> – the amount of times to repeat. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "ᵕ" symbol instead of underscores in <text>!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#targets)

*   Texts.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to quickly and easily set the lore of the item with already existing lore through the [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action, you can use this placeholder to repeat "|" symbol (new line symbol in the "lore" option in the "change\_item" action) as many times as the current lore length, using the [item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
 placeholders to check the lore length. This is not the only way to do it, but still may be useful.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_Hello_5% # Repeat the "Hello" word 5 times

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_|_{CEP_item_loreAmount_HAND}% # Repeat the "|" symbol as many times as lore length of the item in the player's hand (see "Where is useful" for more info)

# Placeholder for random block in area | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#meaning)

Allows you to get a random block in the specified area, using the many different useful options and filters.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#format)

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_<world>_<minX>_<minY>_<minZ>_<maxX>_<maxY>_<maxZ>_<output1>_<output2>_<outputN>_(optional) <filters>_(optional) highest-|+<number>_(optional) blocks=<block1>,<block2>,<blockN>;block-data=<block_data1>|<block_data2>|<block_dataN>;coords=<location1>|<location2>|<locationN>%

<world>\_<minX>\_<minY>\_<minZ>\_<maxX>\_<maxY>\_<maxZ> – the area to choose the block from; (MANDATORY)

<outputs> – may be type, x, y, z or world (you can combine them via "\_", but at least one should exists); (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be solid, fluid or !air (you can combine them via "\_" too); (OPTIONAL)

highest-|+<number> – allows you to specify at what height you want to search for a block, starting from the highest block in the specified area, before the number comes the sign + or -, then the number itself, the highest blocks in the specified area can be many, and if starting from it, adding your number, there will be a suitable block, it will be selected; (OPTIONAL)

blocks=<block1>,<block2>,<blockN>;block-data=<block\_data1>|<block\_data2>|<block\_dataN>;coords=<location1>|<location2>|<locationN> – the additional filters, their order and presence is not important, the main thing is to separate them by semicolons, you can use the “contains”, “startsWith”, “endsWith” and their !-versions in the "blocks" and "block-data", but not in the "coords"! You can use everywhere "!" before something to exclude it, and this is already available in "coords". If you choose not to specify “contains” and the like in "block-data", but a full expression with ! or not, you need to specify the full data format as minecraft:<block>\[<data>=<value>\]. You can use "~" to specify the coordinate ranges in the "coords", you can exclude coordinates from the current range or add coordinates outside the current range, and coordinates added in the current range will take precedence over those excluded in the current range. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <block-data> and <coords> additional filters!

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#big-but-important-information)

Big but important information:

triangle-exclamation

If no filters are specified, all blocks will be taken into account. If filters like blocks= are specified, and no regular filters, they should contain at least one positive value, otherwise no blocks will be taken into account. If regular filters are specified too, then positive blocks= and block-data= will be added to them, and negative ones will be excluded (this means that if you specify, for example, filter solid, and in blocks=, for example, STONE, nothing will change, because solid already contains this type of block, only, for example, specifying !STONE, that is, excluding it from the list, will matter, or, for example, if you specify fluid and add STONE to it, will matter too). That is, the MAIN RULE of filters is that every POSITIVE filter is ADDED to the total list of blocks in the range, not exclude everything else, and every NEGATIVE filter is EXCLUDED and takes into account other filters, for example: blocks=contains CAMPFIRE;block-data=contains lit=true - will take ALL campfires and ALL blocks with lit=true in the data (that is, torches too etc). If you want to take ONLY CAMPFIRES with lit=true, you should specify like: blocks=contains CAMPFIRE;block-data=!contains lit=false - this will take ALL blocks with lit=true in the data and select ONLY CAMPFIRES from them (this is not the only way of such selection, but it is one of the most reliable and easy to understand). Specifying the highest- will have the almost highest priority between all filters, and only coords= will be the highest, overriding all possible options, adding or excluding coordinates from the list.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#targets)

*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in creating some mini-games with random blocks choosing and in many other cases.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_{player_world}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}+5}_type_x_y_z_!air_solid_fluid_highest-3_blocks=!DIRT,!ANDESITE% # Output the type and coordinates of a random block within 5 blocks radius of the current player, excluding air, including solid and liquid blocks, at a height of -3 blocks from some highest block, excluding dirt and andesite, that is, it can be, for example, stone, water, lava etc

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_{player_world}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}+5}_type_x_y_z_blocks=endsWith WOOL,!startsWith L;block-data=contains lit=true;coords=coords=!world,53,23,424~47,19,418|world,52,22,422|testᵕworld,10,52,1152% # Output the type and coordinates of a random block within 5 blocks radius of the current player, including only wool which is not starting with "L" letter, also including any blocks with data "lit=true", excluding the specified range of coordinates from the current search, including one block back from that range and including one block from world test_world (that is, significantly another location), that is, it can be, for example green wool, orange wool, campfires, torches and some different blocks by coordinates

# Placeholder for random block in area | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#meaning)

Allows you to get a random block in the specified area, using the many different useful options and filters.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#format)

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_<world>_<minX>_<minY>_<minZ>_<maxX>_<maxY>_<maxZ>_<output1>_<output2>_<outputN>_(optional) <filters>_(optional) highest-|+<number>_(optional) blocks=<block1>,<block2>,<blockN>;block-data=<block_data1>|<block_data2>|<block_dataN>;coords=<location1>|<location2>|<locationN>%

<world>\_<minX>\_<minY>\_<minZ>\_<maxX>\_<maxY>\_<maxZ> – the area to choose the block from; (MANDATORY)

<outputs> – may be type, x, y, z or world (you can combine them via "\_", but at least one should exists); (MANDATORY)

<filters> – may be solid, fluid or !air (you can combine them via "\_" too); (OPTIONAL)

highest-|+<number> – allows you to specify at what height you want to search for a block, starting from the highest block in the specified area, before the number comes the sign + or -, then the number itself, the highest blocks in the specified area can be many, and if starting from it, adding your number, there will be a suitable block, it will be selected; (OPTIONAL)

blocks=<block1>,<block2>,<blockN>;block-data=<block\_data1>|<block\_data2>|<block\_dataN>;coords=<location1>|<location2>|<locationN> – the additional filters, their order and presence is not important, the main thing is to separate them by semicolons, you can use the “contains”, “startsWith”, “endsWith” and their !-versions in the "blocks" and "block-data", but not in the "coords"! You can use everywhere "!" before something to exclude it, and this is already available in "coords". If you choose not to specify “contains” and the like in "block-data", but a full expression with ! or not, you need to specify the full data format as minecraft:<block>\[<data>=<value>\]. You can use "~" to specify the coordinate ranges in the "coords", you can exclude coordinates from the current range or add coordinates outside the current range, and coordinates added in the current range will take precedence over those excluded in the current range. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <block-data> and <coords> additional filters!

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#big-but-important-information)

Big but important information:

triangle-exclamation

If no filters are specified, all blocks will be taken into account. If filters like blocks= are specified, and no regular filters, they should contain at least one positive value, otherwise no blocks will be taken into account. If regular filters are specified too, then positive blocks= and block-data= will be added to them, and negative ones will be excluded (this means that if you specify, for example, filter solid, and in blocks=, for example, STONE, nothing will change, because solid already contains this type of block, only, for example, specifying !STONE, that is, excluding it from the list, will matter, or, for example, if you specify fluid and add STONE to it, will matter too). That is, the MAIN RULE of filters is that every POSITIVE filter is ADDED to the total list of blocks in the range, not exclude everything else, and every NEGATIVE filter is EXCLUDED and takes into account other filters, for example: blocks=contains CAMPFIRE;block-data=contains lit=true - will take ALL campfires and ALL blocks with lit=true in the data (that is, torches too etc). If you want to take ONLY CAMPFIRES with lit=true, you should specify like: blocks=contains CAMPFIRE;block-data=!contains lit=false - this will take ALL blocks with lit=true in the data and select ONLY CAMPFIRES from them (this is not the only way of such selection, but it is one of the most reliable and easy to understand). Specifying the highest- will have the almost highest priority between all filters, and only coords= will be the highest, overriding all possible options, adding or excluding coordinates from the list.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#targets)

*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in creating some mini-games with random blocks choosing and in many other cases.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-random-block-in-area#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_{player_world}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}+5}_type_x_y_z_!air_solid_fluid_highest-3_blocks=!DIRT,!ANDESITE% # Output the type and coordinates of a random block within 5 blocks radius of the current player, excluding air, including solid and liquid blocks, at a height of -3 blocks from some highest block, excluding dirt and andesite, that is, it can be, for example, stone, water, lava etc

Copy

    %CEP_randomBlock_{player_world}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}-5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_x}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_y}+5}_{math_0:DOWN_{player_z}+5}_type_x_y_z_blocks=endsWith WOOL,!startsWith L;block-data=contains lit=true;coords=coords=!world,53,23,424~47,19,418|world,52,22,422|testᵕworld,10,52,1152% # Output the type and coordinates of a random block within 5 blocks radius of the current player, including only wool which is not starting with "L" letter, also including any blocks with data "lit=true", excluding the specified range of coordinates from the current search, including one block back from that range and including one block from world test_world (that is, significantly another location), that is, it can be, for example green wool, orange wool, campfires, torches and some different blocks by coordinates

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for the highest block at a locationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-the-highest-block-at-a-location)
[NextPlaceholder for biome by coordinateschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-biome-by-coordinates)

# Placeholder for Bedrock state for offline players | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-bedrock-state-for-offline-players#meaning)

Allows you to check whether the online players or offline players are Bedrock players or not, because %floodgate\_isbedrock% placeholder from Floodgate plugin is working only for online players.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-bedrock-state-for-offline-players#format)

Copy

    %CEP_isBedrock_<uuid>%

<uuid> – UUID of the player. (MANDATORY)

* * *

* * *

For example, when you need to check in ConditionalEvents "player\_pre\_join" event whether the player is Bedrock player or not by its uuid (because only uuid is available there).

* * *

    %CEP_isBedrock_c7026d01-d7c9-4e83-8594-60a9aa450f02% # Get "true" or "false" depends on this is Bedrock player or not

# Placeholder for different information about EssentialsX warps | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**ESSENTIALSX**arrow-up-right](https://essentialsx.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps#meaning)

Allows you to get different information about EssentialsX warps since the EssentialsX has not any placeholders like that.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps#format)

Copy

    %CEP_warps_<info>_<separator>_(optional) <warp>%

<info> – the information to get, may be (for some informations see more info in the hint): (MANDATORY)

*   isWarp
    
*   isEmpty
    
*   loc:<(optional, in any order) world,x,y,z>
    
*   owner:<uuid | type | enum | name | coords>
    
*   list
    
*   amount
    

<separator> – the separator to separate the elements in different cases, it is needed when more than one element is outputting, for example in "owner" with "coords" output type, or in "loc", or in "list"; (MANDATORY)

<warp> – the warp to get the information about (you can skip it in case of "isEmpty", "list" and "amount" options); (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-info

The "isWarp" option will check whether the provided name is the existed warp.

The "isEmpty" option will check whether the Essentials file with warps is empty or not.

The "loc" option will output the location of the warp.

The "owner" option will output chosen information about the warp owner ("coords" only for online players).

The "list" option will output the list of existed warps.

The "amount" option will output the amount of existed warps.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps#targets)

*   Warps.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to obtain some information about some warp for your systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-information-about-essentialsx-warps#examples)

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for real nickname in Essentials based on custom nicknamechevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname)
[NextIndependent placeholderschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    %CEP_warps_isWarp_,_abc% # Check whether the "abc" is a real warp

Copy

    %CEP_warps_loc:world,y_|_megaWarp% # Output the world and the Y coordinate of the "megaWarp" warp through the "|" symbol

Copy

    %CEP_warps_list_,% # Output the list of existed warps through the comma

# change_spawner | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner#meaning)

Allows you to change different options of spawners, for example entity type in spawner, or spawn delay, or any other different spawner rules.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner#format)

Copy

    - 'change_spawner: <option>;<value>;<world,x,y,z>'

<option> – may be (for some actions see more info in the hint): (MANDATORY)

*   spawnerType
    
*   spawnerDelay
    
*   spawnerRequiredPlayerRange (alias: spawnerReqPlRng)
    
*   spawnerSpawnRange (alias: spawnerSpRng)
    
*   spawnerMaxNearbyEntities (alias: spawnerMaxNEnt)
    
*   spawnerMaxSpawnDelay (alias: spawnerMaxSpDel) – **should be above zero and greater or equal to spawnerMinSpawnerDelay!**
    
*   spawnerMinSpawnDelay (alias: spawnerMinSpDel)
    
*   spawnerSpawnCount (alias: spawnerSpCount)
    

<value> – the value for the option, always integer except "spawnerType" option, in which should be entity type; (MANDATORY)

<world,x,y,z> – the location of the block. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-info

The "spawnerType" option sets the entity type the spawner is set to spawn.

The "spawnerDelay" option sets the current countdown (in ticks) until the next spawn attempt.

The "spawnerRequiredPlayerRange" option sets the activation radius (in blocks) a player must be within for the spawner to work.

The "spawnerSpawnRange" option sets the radius (in blocks) around the spawner where mobs can appear.

The "spawnerMaxNearbyEntities" option sets the maximum number of nearby same-type entities allowed before spawning is blocked.

The "spawnerMaxSpawnDelay" option sets the maximum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerMinSpawnDelay" option sets the minimum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerSpawnCount" option sets how many entities are spawned per spawn attempt.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner#targets)

*   Blocks ([BaseSpawnerarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/spawner/BaseSpawner.html)
    , [Spawnerarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/spawner/Spawner.html)
    , [CreatureSpawnerarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/CreatureSpawner.html)
    ).
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to change the spawner in the world.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_spawner#examples)

Copy

    - 'change_spawner: spawnerRequiredPlayerRange;40;world,10923,71,3595' # Change the spawner's "required player range" setting

Copy

    - 'change_spawner: spawnerType;CREEPER;world,432,54,1845' # Change the spawner's "entity type" setting

* * *

[Previousmanage\_cyclechevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/manage_cycle)
[NextPlaceholderschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders)
