# Placeholder for custom data | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#meaning)

Allows you to save, delete and obtain variables for players, coordinates, entities and global state (in a file or temporarily).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#format)

Copy

    %CEP_customData_<action>_<name>_(semi-mandatory) <data>_(optional) <entity_uuid|player_name|player_uuid|world,x,y,z>%

<action> – may be set, remove, get, getset, increase, decrease, multiply or divide, "getset" is needed to get a variable if it exists or set it if it does not exist, "increase", "decrease" "multiply" and "divide" are needed for the numerical values to perform mathematic operations on them, before the action you can write “temp” (for example: "tempset"), then instead of perpetual variables temporary variables will be used, which will be stored until the server restarts; (MANDATORY)

<name> – the name of the variable (do not use underscores); (MANDATORY)

<data> – the data to save in the variable (only in case of "set", "getset", "increase", "decrease" "multiply" and "divide" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuid | player\_name | player\_uuid | world,x,y,z> – the target which own the variable (if no target is specified, a global variable will be used). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**Be careful while specifying nicknames of offline players, this can cause a small lag! Better use UUIDs instead.**

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <data>!

circle-exclamation

The perpetual variables and temporary variables are different! The same variables names will point to different variables.

circle-exclamation

You will get back the specified or saved data in any case, nevermind using the "get" or "set". In case of "remove" you will get "true" or "false" depending on the removing result. In case of "increase", "decrease" "multiply" or "divide" you will get back the result of the operation or "NotANumber" if your data or saved data is not a number or does not exist.

You can also use [Stringarrow-up-right](https://github.com/PlaceholderAPI/PlaceholderAPI/wiki/Placeholders#string)
 expansion from PlaceholderAPI and its "%string\_substring\_<startIndex>,<endIndex>\_<string>%" placeholder to trim your data placeholder to the zero characters if you do not want to get the data back.

circle-info

If "temp" prefix will not be specified in the action, the variable will be stored in a file at the path plugins/TriggerReactor/var.json (you can change this file, changes will take effect after the command /trg reload confirm), otherwise the variable will be stored in the server memory until it is restarted.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in many cases to save, change, delete and obtain different data for different objects in a comfortable way. It can be used in many different systems and mini-games.

For example, in ConditionalEvents conditions, when you need to use %random\_<min>\_<max>% placeholder and save its output right in the conditions for further using without regenerating the random number.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_customData_set_coins_2_{player}% # Set some "coins" data to "2" for the current player 

Copy

    %CEP_customData_tempgetset_taxes_100_world,643,54,1542% # Set temporary variable as some "taxes" data if it does not exist to "100" or get the current value otherwise for some block at the location 

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for different team information (/team)chevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team)
[NextPlaceholder for different entity informationchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for custom moon phases | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#meaning)

Allows you to get custom moon phases in the night, for example when moon is on the top, it will be "FULL MOON".

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#format)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_<customState (true|false)>:(semi-optional) <customOutputs>_<world>%

<customState> – the state whether to get the number of the phase (**from 0 to 7**) or its appropriate name; (MANDATORY)

<customOutputs> – the custom output settings, that is how current output will be changed, **you can combine them via comma** (**use only in "true" case of the "customState" option**); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#the-customoutputs-possible-settings-by-default-english-words-with-spaces)

The "customOutputs" possible settings (by default - English words with spaces):

Us

Dh

Lc

Uc

FUc

ES

RU

EN

Replace spaces between words with underscores

Replace spaces between words with dashes

Lowercase all words

Uppercase all words

Uppecrase only first letter of each word

Spanish words

Russian words

English words

<world> – the world from which get the moon. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Note that the language custom output will override all already applied outputs, if specified at the end, **use language custom outputs at the start**!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#targets)

*   Worlds.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#where-is-useful)

It can be useful, for example, to add some more realism to the game, or implement some of your "role-playing" features.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_true:ES,Us,FUc_world% # Get the custom named moon phase in the world "world", in Spanish, underscoring spaces between words and uppercase only first letter of each word, for example "Luna_Creciente"

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_false_test_world% # Get the moon phase in the world "test_world", in number, for example 5

[PreviousPlaceholder for custom player listschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)

# Placeholder for working with MySQL | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#meaning)

Allows you to work with MySQL and other external databases, using the JDBC link for the connection and performing different queries using PreparedStatement (default queries are suitable too).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#format)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_<connection_method>_(semi-mandatory) <jdbc_url>_(semi-mandatory) <sql_query>_(semi-mandatory) <param1>,<param2>,<paramN>%

<connection\_method> – the method to connect to the database through, may be SYNC or ASYNC, in case of "ASYNC" use format "ASYNC:<key>", you can just specify the "key" to get the data by it, or the full placeholder to save the data to this "key" (see more in the hint); (MANDATORY)

<jdbc\_url> – the JDBC link to connect to the database (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<sql\_query> – the query to the database (only obtaining the data) (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<params> – the substitutes for the "?" in the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query" (use it only in case if you are using the PreparedStatements in the "sql\_query") (mandatory in case of "SYNC" <connection\_method> and optional in case of "ASYNC"). (SEMI-MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores and "╵" symbol instead of percents everywhere! Only <connection\_method> is unaffectable, do not use underscores and percents in it at all.

circle-exclamation

"ASYNC" <connection\_method> allows you to return data asynchronously, you will get nothing from the common returning placeholder, it will just save the data to the specified key, only on the next time (for example, after one or more ticks delay), using the partial returning placeholder (that is, only <connection\_method>) you will get the data by the specified key. "SYNC" <connection\_method> works as usual, but it can load the server performance more!

circle-info

Not only PreparedStatements are available, default queries are suitable too.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#targets)

*   SQL queries.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to obtain data from the external databases in any way.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_SYNC_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Get three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" in a synchronous way

Copy

    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test_jdbc:mysql://u256340ᵕPIuNdnjIDAD:0gwDfoEdN╵44ySggXPCF╵2B56uFLpC39za╵5E@mysql-org-d1.test.xyz:3306/s263450ᵕTESTDB_SELECT * FROM TestTable WHERE Player = ? AND Action = ? ORDER BY ID DESC LIMIT ?_0ptifyne,ObtainingMoney,3% # Save three last entries from the TestTable with player "0ptifyne" and action "ObtainingMoney" to the specified key in a asynchronous way
    # After one or more ticks delay
    %CEP_mysql_ASYNC:test% # Get the saved value by the specified key in previous placeholder

* * *

circle-info

Note that any external databases are suitable, not just MySQL.

[PreviousPlaceholder for different block informationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information)
[NextPlaceholder for checking structureschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures)

# Placeholder for repeating the text | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#meaning)

Allows you to repeat the text as many times as you will specify.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#format)

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_<text>_<amount>%

<text> – the text to repeat; (MANDATORY)

<amount> – the amount of times to repeat. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "ᵕ" symbol instead of underscores in <text>!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#targets)

*   Texts.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to quickly and easily set the lore of the item with already existing lore through the [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action, you can use this placeholder to repeat "|" symbol (new line symbol in the "lore" option in the "change\_item" action) as many times as the current lore length, using the [item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-items)
 placeholders to check the lore length. This is not the only way to do it, but still may be useful.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_Hello_5% # Repeat the "Hello" word 5 times

Copy

    %CEP_repeat_|_{CEP_item_loreAmount_HAND}% # Repeat the "|" symbol as many times as lore length of the item in the player's hand (see "Where is useful" for more info)

[PreviousPlaceholder for checking structureschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures)
[NextPlaceholder for custom player listschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)

# Placeholder for custom moon phases | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#meaning)

Allows you to get custom moon phases in the night, for example when moon is on the top, it will be "FULL MOON".

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#format)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_<customState (true|false)>:(semi-optional) <customOutputs>_<world>%

<customState> – the state whether to get the number of the phase (**from 0 to 7**) or its appropriate name; (MANDATORY)

<customOutputs> – the custom output settings, that is how current output will be changed, **you can combine them via comma** (**use only in "true" case of the "customState" option**); (SEMI-OPTIONAL)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#the-customoutputs-possible-settings-by-default-english-words-with-spaces)

The "customOutputs" possible settings (by default - English words with spaces):

Us

Dh

Lc

Uc

FUc

ES

RU

EN

Replace spaces between words with underscores

Replace spaces between words with dashes

Lowercase all words

Uppercase all words

Uppecrase only first letter of each word

Spanish words

Russian words

English words

<world> – the world from which get the moon. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Note that the language custom output will override all already applied outputs, if specified at the end, **use language custom outputs at the start**!

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#targets)

*   Worlds.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#where-is-useful)

It can be useful, for example, to add some more realism to the game, or implement some of your "role-playing" features.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-moon-phases#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_true:ES,Us,FUc_world% # Get the custom named moon phase in the world "world", in Spanish, underscoring spaces between words and uppercase only first letter of each word, for example "Luna_Creciente"

Copy

    %CEP_customMoon_false_test_world% # Get the moon phase in the world "test_world", in number, for example 5

[PreviousPlaceholder for custom player listschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-player-lists)
[NextPlaceholder for Bedrock state for offline playerschevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-bedrock-state-for-offline-players)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for custom data | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#meaning)

Allows you to save, delete and obtain variables for players, coordinates, entities and global state (in a file or temporarily).

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#format)

Copy

    %CEP_customData_<action>_<name>_(semi-mandatory) <data>_(optional) <entity_uuid|player_name|player_uuid|world,x,y,z>%

<action> – may be set, remove, get, getset, increase, decrease, multiply or divide, "getset" is needed to get a variable if it exists or set it if it does not exist, "increase", "decrease" "multiply" and "divide" are needed for the numerical values to perform mathematic operations on them, before the action you can write “temp” (for example: "tempset"), then instead of perpetual variables temporary variables will be used, which will be stored until the server restarts; (MANDATORY)

<name> – the name of the variable (do not use underscores); (MANDATORY)

<data> – the data to save in the variable (only in case of "set", "getset", "increase", "decrease" "multiply" and "divide" actions); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<entity\_uuid | player\_name | player\_uuid | world,x,y,z> – the target which own the variable (if no target is specified, a global variable will be used). (OPTIONAL)

* * *

triangle-exclamation

**Be careful while specifying nicknames of offline players, this can cause a small lag! Better use UUIDs instead.**

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <data>!

circle-exclamation

The perpetual variables and temporary variables are different! The same variables names will point to different variables.

circle-exclamation

You will get back the specified or saved data in any case, nevermind using the "get" or "set". In case of "remove" you will get "true" or "false" depending on the removing result. In case of "increase", "decrease" "multiply" or "divide" you will get back the result of the operation or "NotANumber" if your data or saved data is not a number or does not exist.

You can also use [Stringarrow-up-right](https://github.com/PlaceholderAPI/PlaceholderAPI/wiki/Placeholders#string)
 expansion from PlaceholderAPI and its "%string\_substring\_<startIndex>,<endIndex>\_<string>%" placeholder to trim your data placeholder to the zero characters if you do not want to get the data back.

circle-info

If "temp" prefix will not be specified in the action, the variable will be stored in a file at the path plugins/TriggerReactor/var.json (you can change this file, changes will take effect after the command /trg reload confirm), otherwise the variable will be stored in the server memory until it is restarted.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#targets)

*   Players;
    
*   Entities;
    
*   Blocks.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#where-is-useful)

Can be useful in many cases to save, change, delete and obtain different data for different objects in a comfortable way. It can be used in many different systems and mini-games.

For example, in ConditionalEvents conditions, when you need to use %random\_<min>\_<max>% placeholder and save its output right in the conditions for further using without regenerating the random number.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-custom-data#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_customData_set_coins_2_{player}% # Set some "coins" data to "2" for the current player 

Copy

    %CEP_customData_tempgetset_taxes_100_world,643,54,1542% # Set temporary variable as some "taxes" data if it does not exist to "100" or get the current value otherwise for some block at the location 

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for different team information (/team)chevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-team-information-team)
[NextPlaceholder for different entity informationchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for replacing input through the RegEx | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex#meaning)

Allows you to replace input through the RegEx in convenient and multifunctional way.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex#format)

Copy

    %CEP_replaceRegEx_<pattern>_<replace>_<input>%

<pattern> – the RegEx pattern to apply it for replacion (you can use AIs or any suitable sites for generating it); (MANDATORY)

<replace> – the value to which replace the pattern; (MANDATORY)

<input> – the input for replacion. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

**You can use** **everywhere****:**

Useful for RegEx patterns where you do not want so that {} will be parsed as placeholder, but will be a part of the pattern:

*   "ᵕ" symbol to replace to "\_" symbol
    
*   "╵" symbol to replace to "%" symbol
    
*   "<" symbol to replace to "{" symbol
    
*   ">" symbol to replace to "}" symbol
    

Also useful for RegEx patterns where you do not want so that {} will be parsed as placeholder and will be a part of the pattern, but will be a part of the search symbols in pattern:

*   "\\ᵕ" symbol to replace to escaped "\\\_" symbol
    
*   "\\╵" symbol to replace to escaped "\\%" symbol
    
*   "\\<" symbol to replace to escaped "\\{" symbol
    
*   "\\>" symbol to replace to escaped "\\}" symbol
    

Useful where you not need to replace these symbols but use the original symbols:

*   "\\\\ᵕ" symbol to replace to the original "ᵕ" symbol
    
*   "\\\\╵" symbol to replace to the original "╵" symbol
    
*   "\\\\<" symbol to replace to the original "<" symbol
    
*   "\\\\>" symbol to replace to the original ">" symbol
    

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex#targets)

*   Strings.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex#where-is-useful)

For example, if you want to replace many different parts of some message with any difficilty level at the same time efficiently and easily.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-regex#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_replaceRegEx_^(\d<4>)\s?(\d<4>)\s?(\d<4>)\s?(\d<4>)$_**** **** **** $4_1234 5678 9012 3456% # Hide the bank card first numbers, so that it will be "**** **** **** 3456"

Copy

    %CEP_replaceRegEx_\b(hello|yeah)\b_word_hello, man! yeah... yes?% # Replace all "hello" and "yeah" words in message with "word" word, so that it will be "word, man! word... yes?"

[PreviousPlaceholder for checking whether the input can be an instance of a different objectschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-whether-the-input-can-be-an-instance-of-a-different-objects)
[NextPlaceholder for replacing input through the multi replacementchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-replacing-input-through-the-multi-replacement)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for LuckPerms permissions with contexts | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

triangle-exclamation

**YOU NEED THE** [**LUCKPERMS**arrow-up-right](https://luckperms.net/)
 **PLUGIN FOR THIS TO WORK.**

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#meaning)

The usual LuckPerms placeholders do not allow you to check permission with specific contexts. With this placeholder you can check for context specific permissions for both groups and players.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#format)

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#check-presence-of-permission)

Check presence of permission:

Copy

    %CEP_lp_has_permission_in_contexts_<player|player_uuid|group>_<permission>_<contexts>% # Check if the permission has the specified contexts

<player | player\_uuid | group> – the group or player to check, **the group should be specified as "group-<group>"** (it supports offline players and underscores in the names as well); (MANDATORY)

<permission> – the permission to check; (MANDATORY)

<contexts> – the contexts of the permission to check, the contexts are specified comma separated, first the context name, then its value with =, for example: server=test,world=nether. (MANDATORY)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#get-contexts-of-permission)

Get contexts of permission:

Copy

    %CEP_lp_get_permission_contexts_<player|player_uuid|group>_<permission>_(optional) <contexts>% # Get all or certain (if specified) contexts of a permission

<player | player\_uuid | group> – the group or player to check, **the group should be specified as "group-<group>"** (it supports offline players and underscores in the names as well); (MANDATORY)

<permission> – the permission to check; (MANDATORY)

<contexts> – the contexts of the permission to get (you can not specify anything to get all contexts, but the last "\_" still should be), the contexts are specified comma separated, and only the names of contexts, without their values, for example: server,world. (OPTIONAL)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "**ᵕ**" symbol instead of underscores in <permission> and <contexts>!

triangle-exclamation

**Be careful while specifying nicknames of offline players, this can cause a small lag! Better use UUIDs instead.**

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#targets)

*   LuckPerms groups;
    
*   Players.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#where-is-useful)

For example, if you need to check if a player has a specified permission in certain contexts, or get contexts of a certain permission from a player.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-luckperms-permissions-with-contexts#examples)

* * *

[PreviousPlugins placeholderschevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders)
[NextPlaceholder for real nickname in Essentials based on custom nicknamechevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/plugins-placeholders/placeholder-for-real-nickname-in-essentials-based-on-custom-nickname)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    %CEP_lp_has_permission_in_contexts_{player}_TestPermission_server=TestServer% # Check if the player has permission with the specified contexts

Copy

    %CEP_lp_get_permission_contexts_{luckperms_primary_group_name}_TestPermission2_% # Get all contexts of the specified permission from the group

# Placeholder for checking structures | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#meaning)

Allows you to get a structure by specifying the location. Also you can check whether is the specified structure exists at the specified location or not.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#format)

Copy

    %CEP_structure_<action>_(semi-mandatory) <structure_type>_<x,y,z,world>%

<action> – the action to perform, may be get or check, "get" will return the structure type at the specified location, and "check" will return whether the structure type at the specified location equals to the specified <structure\_type> option (you can also use "<action>:unsafe:<(optional, by default 10) size>" to use the unsafe mode and its size, see more in the red hint); (MANDATORY)

<structure\_type> – the structure type to compare (use only in case of "check" <action>); (SEMI-MANDATORY)

<x,y,z,world> – the location to check the structure. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-exclamation

Use "-" symbol instead of underscores in <structure\_type>!

triangle-exclamation

This placeholder sometimes may contain strange behavior of structure size/position definition (for example, with some swamp huts). In any "strange" cases (where the structure should be detected, but actually not being detected) you need to try to use "unsafe" option (unsafe because not precise), which will check blocks around in the specified radius (or in 10 blocks radius if radius is not specified), or check blocks around manually (but any way this offset only works inside the current chunk, and not outside).

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#targets)

*   Locations.
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to check structures on a different locations.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-checking-structures#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_structure_get_-5307,72,-6940,world% # Get the sctructure at the specified location

Copy

    %CEP_structure_check:unsafe:15_SWAMP-HUT_1213,54,-440,test_world% # Check whether the sctructure at the specified location is swamp hut or not, also checking all blocks around in 15 radius

* * *

circle-exclamation

The unexplored/unloaded structures are not counted!

triangle-exclamation

This placeholder only works on 1.20.4+ versions!

[PreviousPlaceholder for working with MySQLchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql)
[NextPlaceholder for repeating the textchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-repeating-the-text)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for different block information | CE AAPP v4.0 | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#meaning)

Allows you to get different blocks information, like lighting level, inventory type, size etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#format)

Copy

    %CEP_block_<action>_<separator>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<world>%

<action> – may be (for some actions see more info in the hint): (MANDATORY)

*   light:<fromBlocks | fromSky | default>
    
*   inventory (alias: inv)
    
*   inventorySize (alias: invSize)
    
*   inventoryOwner:<uuid | type | enum | name | coords> (alias: invOwner)
    
*   face
    
*   color:<(may be empty, FRONT by default) side>
    
*   skullOwner:<uuid | type | enum | name | coords>
    
*   skullTexture
    
*   spawnerType
    
*   spawnerDelay
    
*   spawnerRequiredPlayerRange (alias: spawnerReqPlRng)
    
*   spawnerSpawnRange (alias: spawnerSpRng)
    
*   spawnerMaxNearbyEntities (alias: spawnerMaxNEnt)
    
*   spawnerMaxSpawnDelay (alias: spawnerMaxSpDel)
    
*   spawnerMinSpawnDelay (alias: spawnerMinSpDel)
    
*   spawnerSpawnCount (alias: spawnerSpCount)
    

<separator> – the separator to separate the elements in different cases, it is needed when more than one element is outputting, for example in "inventoryOwner" with "coords" output type; (MANDATORY)

<x>\_<y>\_<z>\_<world> – the location of the block. (MANDATORY)

* * *

circle-info

The "light" is for the block light level from blocks, sky or default.

The "inventory" is the type of the current inventory of the block.

The "inventorySize" is the size of the current inventory of the block.

The "inventoryOwner" is the owner of the current inventory of the block.

The "face" will return the block facing, like NORTH or WEST and so on (only for [Directionalarrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/data/Directional.html)
 or [Rotatablearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/data/Rotatable.html)
 blocks like doors, torches etc).

The "color" outputs the blocks color, for example for signs (you can specify the sign side in the <sign> option, see possible values [herearrow-up-right](https://hub.spigotmc.org/javadocs/spigot/org/bukkit/block/sign/Side.html)
).

The "skullOwner" option outputs the chosen information about the head owner (if the player is offline, the "coords" will not be available, if the player also never joined to the server, the "name" will not be available).

The "skullTexture" option outputs the texture value of the head, it requires so that some owner will be present for this head, otherwise the texture will not be obtained (you can read more about all of this in the [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action in "skullTexture" option there).

The "spawnerType" option outputs the entity type the spawner is set to spawn.

The "spawnerDelay" option outputs the current countdown (in ticks) until the next spawn attempt.

The "spawnerRequiredPlayerRange" option outputs the activation radius (in blocks) a player must be within for the spawner to work.

The "spawnerSpawnRange" option outputs the radius (in blocks) around the spawner where mobs can appear.

The "spawnerMaxNearbyEntities" option outputs the maximum number of nearby same-type entities allowed before spawning is blocked.

The "spawnerMaxSpawnDelay" option outputs the maximum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerMinSpawnDelay" option outputs the minimum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerSpawnCount" option outputs how many entities are spawned per spawn attempt.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#targets)

*   Different blocks (depends on the chosen action);
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to get different information about blocks while implementing different systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_block_light:fromBlocks_633_43_234_world% # Get the block lighting level from another blocks at the specified location

Copy

    %CEP_block_inventorySize_1210_75_8534_world1% # Get the block inventory size at the specified location if applicable

* * *

[PreviousPlaceholder for different entity informationchevron-left](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-entity-information)
[NextPlaceholder for working with MySQLchevron-right](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp-v4.0/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-working-with-mysql)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Placeholder for different block information | CE AAPP

* * *

chevron-rightMeaning[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#meaning)

Allows you to get different blocks information, like lighting level, inventory type, size etc.

* * *

chevron-rightFormat[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#format)

Copy

    %CEP_block_<action>_<separator>_<x>_<y>_<z>_<world>%

The "skullOwner" option outputs the chosen information about the head owner (if the player is offline, the "coords" will not be available, if the player also never joined to the server, the "name" will not be available).

The "skullTexture" option outputs the texture value of the head, it requires so that some owner will be present for this head, otherwise the texture will not be obtained (you can read more about all of this in the [change\_item](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/actions/independent-actions/change_item)
 action in "skullTexture" option there).

The "spawnerType" option outputs the entity type the spawner is set to spawn.

The "spawnerDelay" option outputs the current countdown (in ticks) until the next spawn attempt.

The "spawnerRequiredPlayerRange" option outputs the activation radius (in blocks) a player must be within for the spawner to work.

The "spawnerSpawnRange" option outputs the radius (in blocks) around the spawner where mobs can appear.

The "spawnerMaxNearbyEntities" option outputs the maximum number of nearby same-type entities allowed before spawning is blocked.

The "spawnerMaxSpawnDelay" option outputs the maximum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerMinSpawnDelay" option outputs the minimum randomized delay (in ticks) between spawn attempts.

The "spawnerSpawnCount" option outputs how many entities are spawned per spawn attempt.

* * *

chevron-rightTargets[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#targets)

*   Different blocks (depends on the chosen action);
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhere is useful[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#where-is-useful)

Can be useful to get different information about blocks while implementing different systems.

* * *

chevron-rightExamples[hashtag](https://optifynes-organization.gitbook.io/ce-aapp/ce-aapp/placeholders/independent-placeholders/placeholder-for-different-block-information#examples)

Copy

    %CEP_block_light:fromBlocks_633_43_234_world% # Get the block lighting level from another blocks at the specified location

Copy

    %CEP_block_inventorySize_1210_75_8534_world1% # Get the block inventory size at the specified location if applicable
